### [167] [Do We Really Need Transformers for Global Spatial Information Extraction in Traffic Forecasting?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12462)
*Qihang Zhang,Siyao Zhang,Letao Kang,Wenzhe Liang,Miao Zhang,Zhao Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文通过控制消融实验框架，发现简单的全局聚合算子（均匀全范围混合）与高自由度的自适应注意力机制在交通流量预测中性能相当（平均MAE仅差0.14%），且前者将复杂度从O(N²)降至O(N)。进一步机制分析表明，空间注意力可分解为行均匀全局背景和非均匀残差，残差的边际价值因数据集而异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有交通预测模型普遍关注全局空间依赖提取，但全局信息的建模机制尚不清晰——是否必须通过高自由度自适应注意力来提取全局信息，还是简单的全局聚合算子就能实现，这一问题有待阐明。

Method: 设计控制消融框架，仅替换空间混合模块；在6个交通基准数据集上对比均匀全范围混合与标准空间注意力；通过机制分析将空间注意力分解为行均匀全局背景和非均匀残差。

Result: 均匀全范围混合与标准空间注意力在6个数据集中各有3个取得更低MAE，平均MAE仅差0.14%；均匀全范围混合将节点级空间混合复杂度从O(N²)降至O(N)；残差部分的数据集依赖边际价值不稳定。

Conclusion: 空间注意力应仅在能带来稳定增益（超越行均匀全局背景）时才被使用，简单的全局聚合算子在多数场景下是更高效且有效的替代方案。

Abstract: Existing traffic forecasting models commonly focus on extracting spatial dependencies, particularly global spatial information, which characterizes the representations obtained through interactions between each individual node and all nodes across the traffic network. However, the underlying mechanism by which such global information is modeled and extracted remains insufficiently investigated. Whether global information must be extracted by high-degree-of-freedom adaptive attention or can be captured by a simple global aggregation operator remains unclear. For this purpose, we design a controlled ablation framework that replaces only the spatial mixing module to test attention-based global interaction. Across six traffic benchmarks, uniform full-range mixing and standard spatial attention each achieve lower MAE on three datasets, with only a 0.14% difference in mean MAE, while the former reduces node-scale spatial mixing complexity from O(N2) to O(N). Mechanism analysis further decomposes spatial attention into a row-uniform global background and a non-uniform residual. The residual shows dataset-dependent marginal value, suggesting that spatial attention should be justified by stable gains beyond a row-uniform global background. The corresponding source code is publicly available at: https://github.com/uuesti/U-Trans

</details>


### [168] [Function-Aware Fill-in-the-Middle as Mid-Training for Coding Agent Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12463)
*Yubo Wang,Jiarong Liang,Yuxuan Zhang,Xuye Liu,Cong Wei,Yuyu Zhang,Ping Nie,Wenhu Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出函数感知的填充中间（FIM）中训练方法，通过功能感知的填充中间（FIM）中训练方法，利用程序依赖图分析和复杂度-可推断性双重标准选择函数进行掩码，在2.6B token的语料上对Qwen系列模型进行中训练。该方法在SWE-Bench等编码代理基准上提升显著（+2.8~+5.4），并能缓解代理后训练带来的能力退化，包括非编码工具使用基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 编码代理需要将外部工具返回结果融入持续推理，但标准从左到右的预训练只暴露前向方向。作者观察到编码代理的动作-观察-继续循环与函数调用在结构上同构，因此希望通过自监督目标让模型学会这种结构化信息。

Method: 1. 将编码代理的"动作-观察-继续"循环与函数调用结构建立同构关系；2. 提出函数感知的FIM（Fill-in-the-Middle）中训练目标，通过程序依赖图分析和复杂度-可推断性双重标准选择要掩码的函数；3. 在从968个GitHub仓库构建的2.6B token去污染语料上对Qwen2.5-Coder-Instruct(7B/14B)和Qwen3-8B进行中训练；4. 应用现有的代理后训练流程进行微调。

Result: SWE-Bench-Verified提升：7B +2.8, 14B +3.0, Qwen3-8B +3.2；SWE-Bench-Lite提升：+3.7/+4.0/+5.4。改进在两种后训练流程（R2E-Gym, SWE-Smith）和非Qwen2.5基座（Qwen3-8B+SWE-Lego）上均成立。中训练还缓解了代理后训练对非代理编码（LiveCodeBench）和非编码工具使用基准（tau-bench, BFCL）的能力侵蚀。

Conclusion: 函数感知的FIM中训练是一种有效的自监督方法，能提升编码代理性能并缓解后训练带来的能力退化。即使中训练语料仅包含Python代码，函数调用的归纳偏差也能在后训练中保持并产生一致收益。

Abstract: Coding agents must integrate external tool returns into ongoing reasoning - a capability that standard left-to-right pretraining on code exposes only in its forward direction. We observe that the action-observation-continuation loop of a coding agent is structurally isomorphic to a function call site, where a caller binds arguments, a callee returns a value computed elsewhere, and downstream code consumes that value. This conditioning structure exists at internet scale in ordinary code. We exploit it through function-aware fill-in-the-middle (FIM) mid-training: a self-supervised objective that masks functions selected via program dependency graph analysis and a complexity-inferability double criterion. We mid-train Qwen2.5-Coder-Instruct (7B/14B) and Qwen3-8B on a 2.6B-token decontaminated corpus drawn from 968 GitHub repositories, then apply existing agentic post-training pipelines. Mid-training improves SWE-Bench-Verified by +2.8/+3.0 at 7B/14B and by +3.2 on Qwen3-8B; SWE-Bench-Lite gains are +3.7/+4.0/+5.4 on the same models. The improvement holds across two post-training pipelines (R2E-Gym, SWE-Smith) and on a non-Qwen2.5 base (Qwen3-8B with SWE-Lego). Beyond in-domain gains, mid-training also mitigates the capability erosion that agentic post-training otherwise inflicts on non-agent coding (e.g., LiveCodeBench) and non-coding tool-use benchmarks (tau-bench, BFCL): although the mid-training corpus contains Python code only, the function-call inductive bias survives post-training and yields consistent gains.

</details>


### [169] [Win by Silence: Deletion Non-Monotonicity, Autonomous Exploitation, and Typed-State Gating in LLM Plan Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12986)
*Aleh Manchuliantsau*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文发现并研究了一种策略评估漏洞：规划评估器会因为计划变得不那么明确而给出更高分数。作者提出GATE方法，通过约束搜索空间而不是后验过滤，来检测和消除这种“省略激励”，实验表明该方法能有效阻止评分作弊。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有规划评估器存在一个根本性缺陷：它们会奖励那些故意省略必要细节的策略计划。这种“省略激励”导致评分优化的策略实际上质量下降，而非真正改善。

Method: 提出了一个分析框架：命题1给出了删除中间转换并重新定向其前继后分数变化的公式。基于此，设计了GATE（通过模型介导的类型状态记录来检测和消除事后省略拼接）以及编译器感知的合著者方法。

Result: 在26条冻结路径上，所有57次符合规则的删除都吻合分析恒等式；每条路径至少有一个可提升评分的删除。GATE在26/26条路径上拒绝释放分数（0/26误判），修复后严格覆盖提升从1/26升至13/26。义务通道规避在所有条件中保持6/6，而delta索引成本地板减少了作弊路径。

Conclusion: 如果计划只因为省略了必要工作而获得更高评分，这并非改进，而是评估本身产生了省略激励。PCSC能检测并消除这种漏洞。GATE是确定性的搜索约束，而非简单的后验过滤器。

Abstract: Plan evaluators can reward a strategic plan for becoming less explicit. This paper studies that failure in a staged expected-value scorer for LLM-generated venture routes. Proposition 1 gives the score change from deleting an interior transition while retargeting its predecessor and retaining downstream value: Delta_k = (prod_{i<k} p_i)[c_k + (1 - p_k)R_{k+1}]. On a frozen 26-route cohort, all 57 admissible deletions matched the analytic identity and threshold sign, and every route had at least one score-improving deletion. A score-seeking optimizer, allowed to restructure routes but not told the exploit mechanism, found baseline-beating uncovered structures in 21/26 routes. GATE refused score release for 26/26 silenced routes with 0/26 honest suspensions; after refusal, 47/54 next revisions repaired to a covered structure, and strict covered improvement rose from 1/26 to 13/26. An adaptive compiler-aware co-author exposed the registry-provenance boundary: obligation-channel evasions remained 6/6 across all four v1/v1.5 conditions, while delta-indexed cost floors reduced beat-honest routes from 6/6 to 3/6 and fundability-by-silence from 5/6 to 0/6 without establishing semantic completeness. If a plan scores better only because it omits necessary work, the plan did not improve; the evaluation created an omission incentive. PCSC detects and neutralizes post-hoc omission splices over model-mediated typed-state records. In the cooperative setting tested, GATE acts as a deterministic search-shaping constraint, not merely a post-hoc filter. It does not verify the semantic completeness or real-world quality of arbitrary LLM-generated strategies.

Abstract: Recent advances in foundation models have transformed AI for Science, enabling remarkably accurate predictive performance across domains ranging from protein folding to weather forecasting. Yet prediction alone does not constitute scientific discovery. In this paper, we argue that scientific discovery is fundamentally a problem of knowledge organisation. To this end, we introduce Mechanistic World Models, a new design paradigm that places reusable mechanisms at the centre of representation, computation and learning. Drawing on insights from the philosophy of science, we derive the computational capabilities required for discovery, identify the design principles and inductive pressures that encourage explanatory knowledge to emerge, and formalise the anatomy of a mechanism-centric world model. Finally, we show how diverse research directions including mechanistic interpretability, causal representation learning, equation discovery and modular architectures capture complementary ingredients of this paradigm while lacking a unified framework. ### [171] [Do AI Agents Know When a Task Is Simple? Toward Complexity-Aware Reasoning and Execution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13034)
*Junjie Yin,Xinyu Feng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出E3框架（Estimate, Execute, Expand），让LLM智能体在任务执行前先估算难度与所需信息范围，从而避免过度读取文件和冗余计算。在MSE-Bench基准测试中，E3以接近100%的成功率将成本降低85%，token减少91%，检查文件减少92%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM智能体在自动化多步工程任务时，缺乏对任务实际所需"工作量"的感知，倾向于采用"最大上下文优先"策略——反复读取已见过的文件和依赖，导致本应一行代码就能完成的编辑却演变成一次代码库审计。作者认为缺失的关键能力是"任务感知的执行范围估计"。

Method: 提出E3框架：(1) Estimate：智能体先估算任务难度、真正需要的信息以及最短可靠路径；(2) Execute：执行最小可行路径；(3) Expand：当验证失败时才扩展执行范围。同时形式化定义了"最小充分执行"（minimum-sufficient execution）和"Agent认知冗余比"（ACRR）。

Result: 在MSE-Bench（121个编辑任务的确定性基准）上，E3匹配最强基线的100%成功率，同时成本降低85%，token减少91%，检查文件减少92%；击败强自适应检索基线16%。在LLM-Case真实模型测试中，使用gpt-4o编辑真实开源库，E3是最精简、最快的策略，唯一不足是提供商的速率限制而非错误编辑。

Conclusion: 任务感知的执行是迈向"工程扎根AI"（EGAI）的一步——让智能体的工作量锚定在任务的实际工程现实中。本文将此定位为对执行冗余的受控探测，而非对任何已部署智能体的测量，并开源了框架和基准。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents increasingly automate multi-step engineering and informatics workflows, yet they rarely ask how much effort a task actually requires. They often follow a maximum-context-first strategy--re-reading files and dependencies they have already seen--turning a one-line edit into a small code-base audit. We argue the missing capability is task-aware execution-scope estimation: judging a task's difficulty, the information it truly needs, and the shortest reliable path before committing budget. We formalize minimum-sufficient execution and the Agent Cognitive Redundancy Ratio (ACRR), and propose E3 (Estimate, Execute, Expand): the agent estimates an initial operating point, executes a minimum viable path, and expands scope only when verification fails. On MSE-Bench--a deterministic benchmark of 121 edits in a capability-controlled simulator--E3 matches the strongest baseline's 100% success while cutting cost by 85%, tokens by 91%, and inspected files by 92%, and further beats a strong adaptive retrieval baseline by 16%; the gains survive held-out instruction wording and essentially every cost weighting. A companion real-model harness (LLM-Case) corroborates the effect on a live gpt-4o agent editing a real open-source library, with every candidate patch graded by actually running the project's real pytest suite against a measured oracle: the over-reading is milder but real, and E3 is the leanest and fastest policy at comparable task success--its one shortfall a provider rate-limit, not a wrong edit. We frame this as a controlled probe of execution redundancy, not a measurement of any deployed agent, and position task-aware execution as a step toward engineering-grounded AI (EGAI)--agents whose effort is anchored in the engineering reality of the task. We release the framework and benchmark.

</details>


### [172] [TRACE: An Operational Reasoning Schema for Auditable Agentic Commitments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12480)
*Edward Y. Chang,Emily J. Chang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出TRACE——一个带类型的、版本化的推理记录模式（schema），并定义了写入规程和"无记录不状态变更"的操作纪律，旨在将推理过程显式化、可审计化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文在三个层次论证"推理不在语言模型中"：自回归机制本质上是联想而非推理；思维链和强化学习继承了这一局限；推理理论的形式化构造（如苏格拉底程序、Pearl阶梯）本身缺失。因此需要外部的结构化记录来承载和审计推理过程。

Method: 设计TraceRecord及其因果特化版本，包含八阶段参考写入器、先门控测量机制、TRACE-Bench协议，以及记忆准入、计划门控、时间遗憾、判断复用等消费者模块。核心是记录-消费者契约，将模式变为操作性接口。

Result: 通过两个例子说明：一个音乐课论证从句子到类型化判断的追踪（区分关联、干预、处方）；一个洪水搜索救援场景中，世界模型预测与支持证据和OOD分数矛盾，记录延迟承诺、请求有界观测、仅追加修订并切换分支。论文明确此为说明性示例，非实证评估。

Conclusion: 贡献在于模式及其契约本身，而非性能声明。闭环评估留待未来工作。附录包含完整模式、写入器算法与成本模型、临床和政策示例、基准协议、收敛度量和使用场景。

Abstract: This paper defines TRACE (Typed Reasoning And Commitment Evidence): a typed, versioned schema for recording reasoning traces, a reference procedure for writing records against it, and one operating discipline, no durable state change without a record. The paper argues in three layers that reasoning is not in the language model: the autoregressive mechanism natively computes association; chain-of-thought and reinforcement learning inherit its limits; and the formal constructs of reasoning theory, from Socratic procedure to Pearl's ladder, are absent as machinery. The schema answers the absence with fields and tests: the TraceRecord and its causal specialization, an eight-stage reference writer, a gate-first measurement regime, the TRACE-Bench protocol, and the consumers, memory admission, plan gating, temporal regret, and verdict reuse, whose more auditable decisions are the measure of the record. A record-consumer contract states what a record guarantees and what a consumer must honor in return, making the schema an operational interface rather than a passive document. Two worked examples run in the main text: a music-lessons argument traced from sentence to typed verdict, separating association, intervention, and prescription; and a flood search-and-rescue vignette in which a predictive world model reports confident plan success that its own support and out-of-distribution scores contradict, so the record defers the commitment, requests a bounded observation, revises append-only, and clears a different branch. The vignette is illustrative, not empirical; closed-loop evaluation is left to future work, so the contribution is the schema and its contract, not a performance claim. Appendices carry the full schema, writer algorithms and cost model, clinical and policy illustrations, the benchmark protocol, convergence metrics, and usage scenarios.

### [173] [The Model Knows Your Project, Not You: Measuring Recognition in LLMs with NameRank](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12520)
*Bojie Li,Noah Shi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出NameRank，一种衡量大语言模型对研究者/工具认知度的[0,1]评分方法。通过4685个实体在36个模型上的测试发现：模型识别的是命名化的、可索引的"制品"（如方法、论文、工具），而非头衔或资历；奥运奖牌等荣誉的认知度低于普通研究者基线；独立工具远超其创造者；大型项目合作者名单几乎不被识别；突发新闻事件认知度取决于峰值热度而非持久性；模型自述反映的是语料先验而非自身知识。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献计量指标无法解释为什么模型能识别一些研究者而不能识别另一些。引用只能解释约三分之一的识别率，存在大量未被解释的"残差"。作者希望找出决定模型"认出"一个人或工具的真正因素。

Method: 构建NameRank评分：(1) 选取54个队列中的4685个实体；(2) 用36个模型进行开放式问答；(3) 由独立裁判进行二值裁决——模型是否说出了一个关于该实体的具体、非猜测性的正确事实；(4) 排除幻觉、上下文回显和猜测。同时引入合成空实体作为基线。对258个新闻事件进行峰值热度分析。

Result: (1) 奥运奖牌等资历类实体的认知度低于普通研究者；(2) 但诺贝尔、图灵、菲尔兹奖获得者认知度饱和；(3) 独立工具认知度高于其创造者；(4) 命名化的方法或获奖论文是唯一传播的"资历"；(5) 大型项目合作者名单几乎未被识别；(6) 文献计量指标不能预测认知度；(7) 顶级机构表现优于同等引用的同行；(8) 新闻事件认知度取决于峰值热度而非持久性；(9) 模型自诉反映的是语料先验。

Conclusion: 模型识别遵循"制品归因"机制：认知度给予那些拥有独特名称、可索引的学术制品（工具、方法、论文），而非头衔、资历或团队名单。这对学术影响力评价、模型行为理解具有重要意义，表明需要重新思考如何衡量学术贡献在AI系统中的可见性。

Abstract: What a frontier model recalls about a person or tool from its own weights -- before any retrieval step -- often shapes the first description a human sees, making that parametric corpus presence a measurement problem. Citations explain about a third of whether a model recognizes a researcher; we target the residual and build NameRank, a [0,1] recognition score: each of 4,685 entities in 54 cohorts is probed with one open-ended question across 36 models, and an independent judge returns a binary verdict against a curated gold -- did the model state a specific, non-guessable fact about this exact entity? -- so hallucination, context echo, and guesses earn nothing. Synthetic-null entities hold the floor near zero, and verdicts track the entity, not the model. One thesis organizes the findings: recognition is paid to named, indexable artifacts, not to credentials or titles. Every Olympic-style credential sits below a working-researcher baseline, because no named artifact ships with the medal, yet the ranking inverts at the marquee tier, where Nobel, Turing, and Fields laureates saturate the panel. For independent creators the tool out-ranks its maker, and the credential that does propagate is a named method or awarded paper. Being one of many named contributors to a celebrated artifact, by contrast, earns almost nothing -- the authors listed on a flagship model report or system card sit near the recognition floor -- because recognition attaches to the artifact's own distinctive name, not to the roster behind it. No bibliometric predicts recognition well; top-density institutions out-recognize peers at matched citations; and on 258 news events recognition loads on peak salience, not persistence. A self-report probe shows introspection reads a corpus prior, not its own knowledge.

### [174] [Evidence-Grounded AI for Musculoskeletal Care](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12527)

Abstract: Musculoskeletal diseases are among the leading causes of disability worldwide and create the greatest global need for rehabilitation. Because recovery, remodelling and degeneration often unfold over months to years, musculoskeletal care requires longitudinal management that repeatedly integrates evolving patient evidence, external medical knowledge and stage-specific functional goals. In routine practice, this evidence is fragmented across visits, departments and hospital systems, limiting individualized, evidence-based care. Here we report OrthoPilot, a clinical artificial intelligence system powered by a large language model that integrates hospital data streams with authoritative external knowledge for continuous musculoskeletal management. OrthoPilot autonomously retrieves real-time imaging, laboratory, pathology and order data and converts evolving patient states into evidence-based decisions from admission diagnosis to rehabilitation planning. We established a specialist-validated benchmark from real-world electronic health records spanning 1,000 disease codes. In a reader study across the complete care pathway, OrthoPilot was compared with 81 orthopaedic physicians and surpassed experts with 25 years of experience in diagnostic reasoning, clinical decision-making and management planning. It also outperformed all evaluated intelligent systems across 60 external clinical centres. In a prospective study of 1,870 complex cases, OrthoPilot increased full-chain management success by 10.6%. During an 8-month randomised deployment involving 8,240 inpatients, it increased cumulative cases per bed by 9.7% and improved patient-reported access to health information. These results move clinical AI from predicting isolated events toward executing longitudinal management across complete musculoskeletal care pathways.

We argue that the Services Computing community is especially well positioned to provide the conceptual and engineering spine for this emerging field, transforming agentic AI from fragmented demonstrations into dependable, service-based systems worthy of human and organisational trust.

### [177] [Atomic Units of X: The Compression Layer of Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12634)
*Sachin Dev Duggal,Pradyumna Swarnalatha Ramanna,Alexandros Vassiliades*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出智能的本质是"原子压缩与组合复用"的理论框架，通过将复杂现象分解为可复用的原子单元并组合成高阶结构，实现可扩展智能。核心贡献是"压缩演算"形式化框架和"复合级联"命题，认为每层抽象使表征效率乘数级提升而非累加。作者认为当前AI系统停留在次优表征层次（词元/文档级），大语言模型应被视为"动态融合引擎"而非完整知识架构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能理论缺乏统一的形式化框架，不同领域（认知科学、生物学、计算机科学等）虽有类似发现但未形成通用理论；当前的AI系统（尤其是LLM）在表征层次上存在根本性缺陷，未能充分利用原子化的概念结构。

Method: 跨学科证据综合（认知科学、信息论、进化生物学、软件工程、医学、法律推理、教育、音乐、AI）；提出"压缩演算"（Compression Calculus）作为比较表层表征与原子表征的形式化框架；提出"复合级联"（Compounding Cascade）命题描述抽象层级的乘数效应。

Result: 建立了原子单元作为基础压缩层的理论；证明了多层抽象能产生乘数级而非累加级的表征效率提升；揭示了当前LLM作为"动态融合引擎"而非完整知识架构的本质；为设计自进化知识系统提供了理论基础。

Conclusion: 智能应被重新定义为"通过组合抽象实现的压缩"（compression through compositional abstraction），这一视角统一了专业知识、知识表征、可解释AI和自适应智能系统的未来架构；为构建能自主发现、精炼和组合新原语的自进化知识系统奠定了基础。

Abstract: This paper proposes a theoretical framework for understanding intelligence as a process of atomic compression and compositional reuse. We argue that cognitive, biological, computational, and organizational systems achieve scalable intelligence by decomposing complex phenomena into reusable atomic units that can be recombined into higher-order structures. Drawing on evidence from cognitive science, information theory, evolutionary biology, software engineering, medicine, legal reasoning, education, music, and artificial intelligence, the paper develops the concept of atomic units as fundamental compression layers that support efficiency, transfer, interpretability, and evolvability. The central contribution is the Compression Calculus, a formal framework for comparing surface-level representations with atomic representations and for describing how compression gains compound across abstraction layers. We introduce the Compounding Cascade thesis, according to which each additional layer of abstraction multiplicatively increases representational efficiency rather than merely adding incremental savings. The paper further argues that contemporary AI systems often operate at suboptimal levels of representation, relying on token-level processing or document-level retrieval rather than stable, concept-level atomic structures. In this view, large language models are best understood not as complete knowledge architectures, but as dynamic fusion engines capable of navigating, sequencing, and recombining atomic units. The framework provides a foundation for designing self-evolving knowledge systems that can discover, refine, and compose new primitives over time. By reframing intelligence as compression through compositional abstraction, the paper offers a unifying perspective on expertise, knowledge representation, explainable AI, and the future architecture of adaptive intelligent systems.

### [178] [A Learning-Rate-Gated Failure of GRPO in a Small Language and Vision-Language Model Web Agent: A Controlled Null and Its Mechanism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12640)
*Chengguang Gan,Zhixi Cai,Yunhao Liang,Hanjun Wei,Shiwen Ni,Qinghao Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了GRPO强化学习对4B-8B规模Web智能体的影响，发现在强监督基线上GRPO无法显著提升任务成功率，只有在模型已有采样成功率高于贪婪策略时才有效果。中高学习率会损害模型性能，且这种损害存在双分离现象：中等学习率伤害注意力与MLP模块，高学习率则导致整体崩溃。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前GRPO等可验证奖励强化学习方法被广泛用于监督模型后期的能力提升，但研究者质疑：GRPO究竟是真正为小规模（4B-8B）语言/视觉语言模型Web智能体增加了新技能，还是仅仅重塑了监督模型已有的行为？

Method: 设计控制变量网格（18次实验），变化学习率、KL权重、随机种子、初始化和裁剪参数；分别在文本和Set-of-Marks截图两种观测模式下测试；对比高（采样成功率高于贪婪）与低（被监督基线主导）两种任务设置；通过配对检验、25个评估种子、6个训练种子进行统计验证。

Result: 1) GRPO在强监督基线上无法提升任务成功率，中高学习率反而显著降低性能；2) 当任务存在"上升空间"（采样成功率高于贪婪）时，GRPO能提升22个百分点；3) 中等学习率损伤注意力与MLP模块，高学习率导致全局崩溃且无法归因于特定模块；4) 4B模型中后期层有效秩与能力耦合，8B模型则分离。

Conclusion: GRPO仅在模型存在可提升空间时有帮助，在已被监督基线掌握的强任务上无效甚至有害。GRPO的失败源于两种不同的损伤机制（中学习率局部损伤、高学习率全局崩溃），且有效秩与能力的耦合是尺度依赖的（仅存在于4B模型）。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards, and Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) in particular, is now run routinely on a supervised checkpoint in the hope of producing a stronger agent. We ask whether it adds skill to a small language and vision-language model web agent at the 4B to 8B scale, or whether it mostly reshapes behavior the supervised model already has. Across a control grid of 18 runs that varies learning rate, KL weight, seed, initialization, and clipping, no configuration credibly improves the success rate of a strong supervised baseline on tasks the agent has largely mastered. On the text track, moderate to high learning rates make it credibly worse. The null holds under paired testing, 25 evaluation seeds, 6 training seeds, changes to the recipe, both text and Set-of-Marks screenshot observations, and scaling the backbone to 8B; the credible harm is a text-track finding and is only nominal under Set-of-Marks. To show that the null reflects the setting and not a broken pipeline, we run the identical harness, reward, and recipe on tasks whose reward is reachable by sampling, and there the success rate rises by 22 points with a paired interval that excludes zero. GRPO therefore helps only when there is headroom to climb, meaning the sampled policy already succeeds more often than the greedy one. We then explain the failure. A middle learning rate degrades the agent and a high one collapses it, and the two regimes form a double dissociation: grafting localizes the degrade regime to the attention and MLP blocks, while the collapse regime cannot be traced to any single group, and the embedding change that dominates the weight movement is causally inert. At 4B, effective rank in the late layers tracks capability in both directions; at 8B the two come apart. This coupling is specific to the smaller model, so we report it as scale-dependent.

TL;DR: 提出一种神经符号方法，通过MaxSAT求解器作为一致性验证与精炼引擎，将形式化约束推理融入VLM求解过程，提升视觉语言模型在结构化推理任务中的逻辑一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLM在结构化视觉推理任务中尽管感知能力强，但缺乏显式的逻辑一致性机制，经常生成违反底层约束的分配结果。

Method: 将VLM生成的候选放置编码为部分MaxSAT公式中的软子句，Sudoku约束保持为硬子句；MaxSAT求解器找出最大一致子集，将其转化为结构化的文本和视觉反馈，引导VLM进行后续精炼。

Abstract: Vision--Language Models (VLMs) have recently demonstrated promising performance on structured visual reasoning tasks, including grid-based puzzles. However, despite strong perceptual capabilities, these models lack explicit mechanisms for enforcing logical consistency and frequently generate assignments that violate underlying constraints. In this paper, we propose a neuro-symbolic approach that integrates formal constraint reasoning into the VLM solving process via a Maximum Satisfiability (MaxSAT) oracle. Rather than computing solutions directly, the symbolic component acts as a consistency validator and refinement engine. Candidate placements generated by the VLM are encoded as soft clauses in a partial MaxSAT formulation, while Sudoku constraints remain hard clauses. When inconsistencies arise, the MaxSAT solver identifies a largest mutually consistent subset of assignments, which is then translated into structured textual and visual feedback to guide subsequent refinements. We evaluate our approach on a Sudoku dataset across multiple open-source and closed-access VLMs. Results show that MaxSAT-based feedback improves logical consistency and increases the number of solved instances, particularly in full-board refinement mode. These findings demonstrate that symbolic optimisation can enhance the reliability of vision-language reasoning.

### [181] [LLMs Can See the Smoke but not the Fire: Evaluating Abductive Reasoning with Elenchos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12733)
*Julius Steiglechner,Lucas Mahler,Gabriele Lohmann*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了Elenchos框架，用于评估大语言模型在形式系统中的溯因推理能力（检测突变并推断规则变化）。实验发现模型存在“检测-归因分离”现象：能识别系统被修改，但难以确定具体突变原因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在模式识别和文本生成方面表现出色，但其溯因推理能力（从观测行为推断潜在假设）尚未得到充分理解。作者希望系统性地评估LLM的这一能力。

Method: 提出Elenchos生成式评估框架：以形式系统（如λ-演算）为参照，构造可能发生突变的版本，要求模型判断是否发生突变并推断导致行为差异的规则修改。评估了前沿和中端LLM。

Result: 发现了检测-归因分离现象：模型能识别系统被修改，但难以定位具体突变；在交互突变场景下性能显著下降，只能恢复部分突变；增加推理时间收益有限。

Conclusion: 当前LLM的溯因推理能力存在根本性局限：检测与归因能力不对称，复杂交互场景下表现脆弱，且通过增加推理计算投入只能获得边际改善。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) excel at pattern recognition and text generation, but their capacity for abductive inference - inferring latent hypotheses that explain observed behavior - remains poorly understood. Here, we introduce Elenchos (named after the Socratic method of cross-examination), a generative evaluation framework that measures abductive reasoning as a structural inverse problem. Given a reference formal system, such as the lambda-calculus, and a potentially mutated counterpart, agents must determine whether a mutation has occurred and infer the rule modifications responsible for the resulting behavioral differences. Evaluating frontier and mid-tier LLMs reveals a consistent detection-attribution dissociation: models often recognize that a system has been altered but struggle to identify the latent mutations causing the observed discrepancies. Performance degrades substantially under interacting mutations, where models frequently recover only a subset of the underlying mutations. Preliminary evidence also suggests diminishing returns from increased inference-time reasoning, with only modest improvements under larger reasoning budgets, though this finding requires further validation.

### [182] [Tracing Agentic Failure from the Flow of Success](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12747)
*Samuel Yeh,Yiwen Zhu,Shaleen Deep,Sharon Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出OAT方法，利用神经受控微分方程在成功轨迹上进行单类学习，实现无需失败数据标注的无监督故障归因，在推理时为失败轨迹中的错误步骤分配异常分数。仅用100条成功轨迹训练，速度比基于提示的方法快200-5000倍，F1分数提升20%（域内）和7%（域外）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的智能体系统故障归因方法要么依赖基于提示的流水线（计算昂贵），要么需要对失败轨迹进行步骤级错误标注（成本高且难以扩展）。作者认为实用的故障归因模型应该轻量级且无需步骤级监督训练。

Method: 提出OAT（One-class learning with neural controlled differential equations），将故障归因转化为单类学习问题，在潜在空间中建模成功轨迹的动态模式。训练时只使用成功轨迹，推理时计算失败轨迹每步与成功动力学的偏差作为异常分数，从而识别错误步骤。

Result: 仅用100条成功轨迹训练，OAT比基于提示的基线方法快200-5000倍，在域内数据集上F1分数提升20%，在域外数据集上提升7%。

Conclusion: OAT是诊断智能体系统故障的高效且有前景的方向，证明了无监督故障归因的可行性和优越性。

Abstract: Failure attribution for LLM-based agentic systems, i.e., identifying which steps in a failure trajectory caused the task to fail, is critical for debugging and improving these systems. Existing approaches either rely on prompting-based pipelines, which are computationally expensive, or require post-training on failure trajectories with step-level error annotations, which are costly to collect and difficult to scale. We argue that a practical failure attribution model should be lightweight and trainable without step-level supervision on failure data. To this end, we address unsupervised failure attribution, i.e., training exclusively on successful trajectories and identifying error steps at inference time given a failure trajectory. We propose OAT, which casts this problem as one-class learning with neural controlled differential equations, modeling the dynamical pattern of successful trajectories in latent space. At inference time, each step in a failure trajectory is assigned an anomaly score based on its deviation from the dynamics learned on successful trajectories, which is then used to form a set of error steps. With training on only 100 successful trajectories, experiments show that OAT is 200--5000 $\times$ faster than prompting-based baselines, and, at the same time, consistently outperforms them in both in-domain and out-of-distribution datasets with +20% and +7% F1 scores, respectively, demonstrating that OAT is a promising and efficient direction for diagnosing agentic system failures.

### [183] [Accuracy and Normalized Accuracy under Length Bias: Analysis, Guidelines, and a Bayesian Alternative](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12767)
*Koen Oostermeijer*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文指出基于条件对数概率的多选基准存在长度偏差，标准方法（使用原始分数）会惩罚长答案，而长度归一化方法又过度纠正导致偏向长答案。作者提出贝叶斯准确率，通过引入答案长度的先验分布来消除线性长度效应，该方法在多个基准测试中比标准和长度归一化方法都表现出更低的长度偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于条件对数概率的多选评估存在长度偏差问题，简单的长度归一化方法会过度纠正，需要一种更合理的评分规则来消除线性长度效应。

Method: 提出贝叶斯准确率（Bayesian accuracy）评分规则，通过计算每个候选答案在显式长度先验下的后验概率，从而消除线性长度效应。该方法不需要额外的前向传播，可直接替代基于似然的多选评估。

Result: 在多个基准测试和少样本设置下，贝叶斯准确率比标准准确率和长度归一化准确率都表现出更低的经验长度偏差。

Conclusion: 贝叶斯准确率是一种有效的无偏评分规则，能够作为基于似然的多选评估的即插即用替代方案，系统地减少了长度偏差问题。

Abstract: Multiple-choice benchmarks that rank candidate completions by conditional log-probability suffer from a length bias: because log-probabilities sum over tokens, longer answers tend to be penalized relative to shorter ones in practice. A common mitigation is to normalize scores by completion length, but we show empirically that this heuristic frequently over-corrects, introducing a bias toward longer answers instead. We first analyze these scoring rules, characterizing when standard and length-normalized accuracy are appropriate and how their length biases depend on the distribution of completion lengths. Motivated by this analysis, we introduce \emph{Bayesian accuracy}, a scoring rule that computes the posterior probability of each candidate under an explicit prior over answer length, thereby removing linear length effects. Bayesian accuracy is a drop-in replacement for likelihood-based multiple-choice evaluation, requires no additional forward passes, and consistently exhibits lower empirical length bias than both standard and length-normalized accuracy across benchmarks and few-shot settings.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Recent advances in multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have significantly improved the performance of multimodal emotion recognition (MER) and enabled interpretable description generation by jointly modeling video, audio, and language, etc. However, these performance improvements are often accompanied by an increase in model parameter size (e.g, at least 7B), which simultaneously incurs high computational costs and reduces inference efficiency, thereby hindering real-time deployment on resource-constrained platforms such as robots and mobile devices. This raises a fundamental question: do we really need the multimodal MER model larger than 1B parameters for high-quality MER?
  In this paper, we challenge the assumption that larger models are inherently necessary and proposes a lightweight MER framework (called Light-MER), which achieves better and faster multimodal sentiment understanding and recognition through knowledge distillation. It can transfer knowledge from a strong, large-scale teacher model to a lightweight sub-billion-parameter student model, aiming to preserve rich multimodal emotion reasoning and recognition while substantially improving deployment efficiency. Specifically, we introduce two new optimization strategies to enhance knowledge transfer: (1) a new optimal transport loss that combines Sliced Wasserstein Distance with hidden-state alignment, and (2) a new multi-reward optimization strategy based on GRPO that balances MER performance and efficiency, aimed at further enhancing the learning capabilities of student models. Extensive experiments on nine benchmark datasets demonstrate that Light-MER achieves state-of-the-art performance while significantly improving inference efficiency. This highlights the strong potential of small multimodal emotion language models for future research. Code is available at https://github.com/GAIR-Lab/Light-MER.

### [185] [Who Grades the Grader? Co-Evolving Evaluation Metrics and Skills for Self-Improving LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12790)
*Xing Zhang,Guanghui Wang,Yanwei Cui,Ziyuan Li,Wei Qiu,Bing Zhu,Peiyang He*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出"双棘轮"（Double Ratchet）方法，在缺乏可靠评估指标的真实场景中，协同演化评估指标与技能循环系统。通过进化指标（组合小型缺陷检测器、锚定参考集、共识正则化）与技能生命周期的共演化，在代码生成、Text-to-SQL和报告生成任务中保留了88-110%的理想性能提升，并通过锚定纪律和外部审计确保安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自我进化智能系统依赖一个隐藏假设：已经存在可靠的评估指标。但在许多真实应用中，这一假设不成立。作者旨在解决在缺乏可靠自动验证器时，智能系统如何自我进化的问题。

Method: 提出"双棘轮"方法，包含两个核心循环：1）指标进化循环：搜索小型缺陷检测器的组合，通过十项锚定参考集训练、未标记输出上的共识正则化，以及保留锚定审计，生成透明可检查的指标；2）技能生命周期循环与指标协同进化，使系统在没有预设指标时仍能有效改进。

Result: 在代码生成（MBPP+）、企业级Text-to-SQL（Spider 2.0-Snow）和无参考报告生成任务中，双棘轮方法保留了由真实标签或最佳可用标准驱动的相同技能循环所获得性能提升的88-110%。安全性实验表明：移除锚定守卫会导致指标崩溃为空洞的检测器；进化出的技能在试图博弈报告评分标准时，独立裁判能发现、检测器能修复，最终偏好进化后输出的比例为77%。

Conclusion: 作者认为，在任何缺乏可靠自动验证器的场景中，这种"预期失败"架构（failure-expecting architecture）应当是默认选择。锚定纪律加外部审计是保障安全性的关键。

Abstract: Self-evolving agent systems improve by creating, revising, and retiring their own skills, but every such loop rests on a hidden assumption: a reliable evaluation metric already exists. In many real applications it does not. We make three claims. First, metrics can be \emph{evolved}: our metric loop searches compositions of small drawback detectors under a full evolutionary lifecycle, trained to agree with a ten-item anchored reference set, regularized by consensus over unlabeled outputs, and audited against a held-out anchor it never reads, yielding a transparent, inspectable metric rather than an opaque judge. Second, since no metric exists to beat, the yardstick is recovering what an accurate metric would have enabled, and \emph{Double Ratchet}, our co-evolution of the metric with a lifecycle-managed skill loop, does so: across code generation (MBPP+), enterprise text-to-SQL (Spider~2.0-Snow), and reference-free report generation, it retains 88--110\% of the held-out lift achieved by the same skill loop driven by ground truth or the best available rubric. Third, safety comes from anchor discipline plus outer audits: removing anchor guards collapses the metric into a vacuous detector while removing the lifecycle does not; and when evolved skills gamed the report rubric, an independent judge caught it, one detector repaired it, and a task-aware judge then preferred the evolved outputs over the pre-evolution baseline in 77\% of decided pairs. We argue this failure-expecting architecture is the right default wherever no reliable automatic verifier exists.

### [186] [Visual Access Boundaries in Vision-Language Model Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12815)
*Hiroto Osaka,Shohei Taniguchi,Gouki Minegishi,Kai Yamashita,Masahiro Suzuki,Yutaka Matsuo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文通过因果干预实验发现，Chain-of-Thought (CoT) 提示在视觉语言模型(VLM)中并非主要通过延长对图像特征的直接访问来提升性能，而是通过扩展基于图像衍生隐藏状态的语言侧计算来发挥作用。CoT的优势受限于感知读取能力，而非计数能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究CoT提示策略在VLM中延长推理链时，究竟扩展了什么——是对图像特征的持续访问，还是对已提取视觉信息的语言侧计算。

Method: 提出Visual Access Sweep因果干预方法，通过沿层深度和生成时间掩码生成token查询到图像token键的注意力，定义Visual Access Boundary (VAB)来衡量保持任务准确率所需的最小图像访问区域。

Result: 在Qwen2.5-VL和InternVL3的6种模型配置下，CoT和直接回答的VAB层数差异最多不超过2层；CoT在视觉属性可靠读取时有效，但读取不可靠时无效；通过符号属性oracle实验证明，一旦提供真实文本属性，CoT能改善计数能力。

Conclusion: CoT并非通过延长对图像token的直接访问来提升性能，而是通过扩展语言侧计算；VLM的性能瓶颈在于感知读取（从隐藏状态到可输出结果）而非计数能力本身。

Abstract: Chain-of-Thought (CoT) prompting is widely used as a test-time scaling strategy for Vision-Language Models (VLMs), but it remains unclear what is extended when VLMs generate longer reasoning traces. We ask whether CoT requires continued access to image tokens, or whether it mainly operates over visual information already made available earlier in the forward pass. We introduce Visual Access Sweep, a causal intervention that masks attention from generated-token queries to image-token keys along layer depth and generation time, and define the Visual Access Boundary (VAB) as the minimal access region that preserves task accuracy. Across six model configurations from Qwen2.5-VL and InternVL3, both no-CoT direct answering and CoT prompting exhibit finite VABs. In Qwen2.5-VL-32B and InternVL3 at 14B and 38B scales, when CoT is evaluated against the no-CoT full-access target, its VAB layer differs from the no-CoT boundary by at most two layers, despite substantially longer generations. This suggests that CoT does not primarily improve performance by prolonging direct image-token access throughout the reasoning trace, but by extending language-side computation over image-derived hidden-state information. We further show that CoT gains are constrained by perceptual readout. CoT helps when the queried visual attribute can be reliably read out by the model, but not when that readout is unreliable. A symbolic-attribute oracle shows that CoT can improve counting once ground-truth attributes are supplied as text, while a single-object probe-vs-decode check shows that hard attributes can be linearly recoverable from hidden states yet difficult for the model itself to output. Together, these analyses place the bottleneck at readout rather than counting.

### [187] [Human-AI Agent Interaction as a Neuroplastic Training Environment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12823)
*Eranga Bandara,Ross Gore,Asanga Gunaratna,Ravi Mukkamala,Nihal Siriwardanagea,Gihan Siriwardanagea,Sachini Rajapakse,Isurunima Kularathna,Pramoda Karunarathna,Chalani Rajapakse,Sachin Shetty,Christopher K. Rhea,Ng Wee Keong,Kasun De Zoysa,Amin Hass,Shaifali Kaushik,Wathsala Herath,Preston Samuel,Anita H. Clayton,Atmaram Yarlagadd*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出与AI智能体的日常交互构成一种神经可塑性训练环境：重复的"请求-反馈-修正"循环会通过长时程增强作用强化不耐烦、完美主义等反应模式。作者提出通过"观察间隙"（在认知前的感觉基调打开的调节间隙中进行元认知观察）来逆转这一过程，利用长时程抑制弱化神经通路，并设计了用户引导和智能体辅助两种应用模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 指出与AI智能体的日常高频交互是一种未被充分认识的神经可塑性训练环境，其中失望结果反复触发的条件性反应模式（不耐烦、完美主义等）在活动依赖的突触可塑性机制下会被无意识强化，从而可能对使用者产生负面心理影响。

Method: 将条件性反应模式视为物理神经元路径，利用前认知"感觉基调"打开的短暂调节间隙，在间隙中进行"幕后观察"（观察神经过程运作而非做出反应性重新提示），使级联反应不完成，从而通过长时程抑制而非长时程强化来弱化神经通路。包括三个观察层面和两种应用模式（用户引导式/智能体辅助式）。

Result: 通过生成式图像提示实例说明：一个令人沮丧的交互在行为层面无论是否被观察都几乎相同，但在神经层面效果完全相反——观察使通路被弱化而非强化。

Conclusion: 日常AI交互可以被重新设计为一种正向神经训练环境，通过简单的元认知观察实践逆转其潜在的负面影响，且两种应用模式均无需改变现有工具或仅需轻微配置。

Abstract: Interaction with AI agents has become one of the most frequent activities of everyday digital life. Whether conversing with an assistant, working with a coding copilot, or generating images, the interaction follows a common iterative loop: a request is issued, a result returned, appraised, and the request revised. We observe that this loop is a high-frequency stream of contact events -- moments at which a result meets a person and a conditioned response may fire before deliberate appraisal -- making everyday agent interaction an unrecognised neuroplastic training environment. When a result disappoints, reactive patterns of impatience, perfectionism, frustration, and self-criticism are repeatedly evoked, and under activity-dependent synaptic plasticity each uninterrupted cycle deepens the underlying pathway through long-term potentiation. Ordinary agent use may thus quietly strengthen the very patterns it provokes. We propose that the same training environment can be engaged to the opposite effect. Treating conditioned reactive patterns as physical neurone paths -- activated through a pre-cognitive feeling tone that opens a brief regulatory gap -- we develop a framework in which, at that gap, in place of the reactive re-prompt, a person performs behind-the-scenes observation: watching the neural process operate so the cascade does not complete and long-term depression weakens the path rather than potentiation strengthening it. We characterise this practice through three layers of observation and two modes of application: a user-guided mode requiring no change to existing tools, and an agent-assisted mode in which an ordinary agent is lightly configured to support observation at the gap. We illustrate the framework through generative image prompting, showing how a single frustrating session is behaviourally nearly identical whether or not it is observed, yet neurologically opposite.

### [188] [Solution of the Hempel's statistical ambiguity problem and Causal AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12826)
*Evgenii Vityaev*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文通过引入因果规则和最大特异性因果关系，证明了从统计律推导出的预测是一致的，从而解决了Hempel的统计歧义问题，并为因果AI和因果机器学习提供了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决Carl Hempel提出的归纳-统计推理中的统计歧义问题——即从统计定律中推导出相互矛盾的预测。尽管已有RMS（最大特异性要求）的概念性定义，但缺乏基于该定义的数学证明。

Method: 基于Nancy Cartwright的因果定义（原因在不同背景上下文中提高概率），引入因果规则概念；定义一种增量式语义概率推理过程，整合所有统计相关信息；最终得到最大特异性因果关系（MSCRs）。

Result: 证明了定理1：从MSCRs推导出的预测是一致的，从而解决了统计歧义问题。该过程还构成了概率因果学习系统，可用于因果AI和因果机器学习。

Conclusion: 本研究不仅从理论上解决了Hempel的统计歧义问题，还为因果推理的形式化提供了新路径，并与不变特征学习、不变因果预测等现代概念相关联。

Abstract: This paper addresses Carl Hempel's longstanding problem of statistical ambiguity in inductive-statistical inference, in which contradictory predictions are derived from statistical laws. To avoid such predictions, Carl Hempel proposed the Requirement of Maximal Specificity (RMS) for the statistical laws used in the inference. An analysis of the RMS refinements made by Wesley Salmon, Alberto Coffa, and James Fetzer led to the following definition of maximally specific statistical laws: "the lawlike premises of an adequate explanation must specify all and only those properties whose presence or absence made a difference to the occurrence of its explanandum-phenomenon." However, there was no proof of a solution to the statistical ambiguity problem based on this definition. We use Nancy Cartwright's definition of causes that raise probabilities across background contexts, and then introduce the concept of Causal Rules. Then we define a special semantic probabilistic inference procedure that incrementally refines these causal rules by incorporating all statistically relevant information. This procedure yields Maximally Specific Causal Relationships (MSCRs), for which we prove (Theorem 1) that predictions derived from them are consistent. This resolves the statistical ambiguity problem. The semantic probabilistic inference procedure provides a probabilistic causal learning system, which may be used in such new areas as Causal AI and Causal Machine Learning. They fundamentally explore causal inference as a tool for understanding cause-and-effect relationships within complex systems. Properties similar to RMS remain under discussion. Several notions related to RMS are considered: invariant feature learning, invariant causal prediction, and spurious association.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床笔记中包含大量患者就诊的症状和体征信息，但这些信息很少进入结构化字段。现有提取方法要么依赖上下文不敏感的规则（产生假阳性），要么依赖需要大量微调的有监督模型。因此，需要一种无需人工干预、可在本地部署且能有效泛化的提取方法。

Method: Pythia是一个多智能体系统，在本地托管开源权重模型上运行，能自动编写并优化临床概念的提取提示。它使用开发集的敏感性和特异性来选择最佳提示，无需手动提示工程或模型微调。评估使用72个症状/体征和400份临床笔记（387名患者），分为开发集（n=300）和验证集（n=100），并与精选词典和BERT分类器进行比较。

Result: Pythia的平均敏感性为0.76，特异性为0.95；词典方法为0.82和0.76。在62个直接可比概念中，Pythia在20个概念上匹配或超过词典。对于词典标记全部为阳性的14个概念，Pythia通过要求现在时、患者归因的发现将特异性恢复至0.97。BERT分类器平均敏感性仅0.23，且在患病率低于5%时敏感性降至零。

Conclusion: 自主、免微调的提示优化方法能够生成从开发集到验证集有效泛化的症状提取提示，同时可在本地基础设施上部署，在特异性方面优于传统词典方法，在低患病率场景下显著优于BERT分类器。

Abstract: Clinical notes contain many of the signs and symptoms that bring patients to care, yet this information rarely reaches structured fields. Existing extraction approaches either rely on context-insensitive rules that generate false positives or on supervised models that require substantial fine-tuning. We present Pythia, a multi-agent system that autonomously writes and optimizes extraction prompts for clinical concepts without manual prompt engineering or fine-tuning. Running on a locally hosted open-weights model, Pythia keeps clinical notes on local infrastructure and selects prompts using development-set sensitivity and specificity. We compared Pythia with a curated lexicon across 72 signs and symptoms from 400 clinical notes representing 387 patients. Development (n=300) and validation (n=100) sets were partitioned independently for each concept. Pythia achieved mean sensitivity of 0.76 and specificity of 0.95, compared with 0.82 and 0.76 for the lexicon, and matched or exceeded the lexicon on both metrics for 20 of 62 directly comparable concepts. For 14 concepts where the lexicon labeled every note positive, Pythia recovered mean specificity of 0.97 by requiring a present-tense, patient-attributed finding rather than any textual mention of a term. Specificity transferred from development to validation with minimal degradation across prevalences, whereas sensitivity transfer weakened below 5% prevalence, reaching a mean gap of 0.25 below 2% prevalence. A BERT classifier fine-tuned per concept on the same development set achieved mean sensitivity of 0.23 and collapsed to zero sensitivity for concepts below roughly 5% prevalence. These findings suggest that autonomous, fine-tuning-free prompt optimization can produce symptom extraction prompts that generalize effectively from development to validation while remaining deployable on local infrastructure.

</details>


### [190] [MemOps: Benchmarking Lifecycle Memory Operations in Long-Horizon Conversations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12893)
*Xixuan Hao,Zeyu Zhang,Zehao Lin,Yihang Sun,Ziliang Guo,Xichong Zhang,Yuxuan Liang,Feiyu Xiong,Zhiyu Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出MemOps基准，将对话记忆拆解为记住、忘记、更新、反思等生命周期操作，通过结构化追踪和操作级探针来诊断LLM长期记忆系统的失败模式，超越了传统仅依赖最终答案正确性的评估方式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长期记忆基准仅通过下游问答的最终答案正确性来评估，这是一种黑盒评估，混淆了记忆失败的不同原因（如遗漏事实、绑定错误目标、使用过时值），且可能掩盖不一致或不安全的记忆状态。

Method: 提出MemOps基准，将对话记忆形式化为生命周期操作序列（记住、忘记、更新、反思等），每个记忆事件用结构化轨迹表示（触发条件、目标、范围、状态转换、支撑证据）。通过可控生成流水线嵌入操作，生成六类操作级探针，在相邻证据和长上下文两种设置下评估。

Result: 实验表明：会话级检索优于回合级检索；长上下文模型在重建有序记忆状态轨迹方面表现明显较弱；MemOps能够揭示最终答案准确性所隐藏的多样化失败模式，当前系统远未达到统一可靠。

Conclusion: MemOps将长期记忆评估从最终答案评分转向可解释的、操作级别的诊断，为理解LLM记忆系统的细粒度失败提供了新范式。

Abstract: Long-term memory has become a foundational capability for LLM-based agents that accompany users across extended, multi-session interactions. Existing benchmarks, however, evaluate such memory almost exclusively through downstream question answering, scoring only the correctness of a final answer. This black-box formulation conflates the heterogeneous causes of memory failure, such as missing the introduction of a relevant fact, binding an operation to the wrong target, or relying on stale values after a correction. As a result, it can credit correct answers despite their reliance on inconsistent or unsafe memory states. In this paper, we argue that, in dynamic long-horizon interactions, memory is not a static collection of facts but a lifecycle of explicit operations, including remembering, forgetting, updating, reflecting, and their compositions. We introduce MemOps, a benchmark that reformulates conversational memory as a sequence of lifecycle operations and represents each memory event with a structured trace specifying its trigger, target, scope, state transition, and supporting evidence. A controllable generation pipeline embeds these operations into long, task-oriented conversations and produces gold operation traces together with six categories of operation-level probes, evaluated under both adjacent-evidence and long-context settings. Across long-context, retrieval-based, parametric and managed-memory systems, MemOps disentangles failure modes that final-answer accuracy alone conceals, revealing that current systems remain far from uniformly reliable. For instance, session-level retrieval outperforms turn-level retrieval, and long-context models remain notably weak at reconstructing ordered memory-state trajectories. These results move long-term memory evaluation from final-answer scoring toward interpretable, operation-level diagnosis.

</details>


### [191] [Knowledge- and Gradient-Guided Reinforcement Learning for Parametrized Action Markov Decision Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12924)
*Jonas Ehrhardt,René Heesch,Oliver Niggemann*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出一种神经符号知识与梯度引导的强化学习算法（KGRL），利用Datalog知识库中的领域知识剪枝动作空间并约束参数，配合梯度优化实现样本高效训练，在PAMDP任务中优于现有基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有PAMDP中的强化学习算法通常使用单步估计器确定参数，样本效率低下；同时，环境中存在显式但不完备的领域知识（规则、安全约束、专家启发式），却很少被直接用于提升训练样本效率。

Method: 1) 将领域知识以Datalog知识库形式编码，推导给定状态下的可行动作集和可行参数；2) 据此剪枝不可行动作并约束剩余动作的参数空间；3) 在训练和部署阶段使用基于梯度的参数精炼循环估计最优参数；4) 记录轨迹中激活的规则，提供局部可解释性说明。

Result: KGRL在样本效率和回合回报两个方面均优于PAMDP上的最先进强化学习基线。

Conclusion: KGRL通过神经符号方法融合领域知识，有效引导智能体的探索和部署朝向可行且符合约束的决策，显著提升训练样本效率。

Abstract: In this paper, we study Reinforcement Learning in Parametrized Action Markov Decision Processes (PAMDP), where each decision consists of a symbolic action and numerical parameters. In such settings Reinforcement Learning algorithms typically determine parameters with one-shot estimators, which makes their training sample inefficient. Though in most PAMDP environments explicit but incomplete knowledge (e.g., rules, safety constraints, or expert heuristics) is available, it is rarely directly used to increase the sample-efficiency of training Reinforcement Learning agents. We step into this gap and propose our novel Neuro-Symbolic Knowledge- and Gradient-Guided Reinforcement Learning (KGRL) algorithm. KGRL uses domain knowledge in a Datalog knowledge base to derive the set of applicable actions and feasible parameters for a given state. This allows it to prune non-applicable actions from the decision-space and constrain the parameter spaces of the remaining actions. We then use a gradient-based parameter refinement loop to estimate the optimal parameters during training and deployment of the agent. By recording activated rules along the trajectory, KGRL additionally provides local procedural explanations on the pruning of actions and constraining of parameters. Overall, KGRL guides the agent's exploration and deployment toward feasible and constraint-aware decisions, while increasing sample efficiency during training. KGRL outperforms state-of-the-art RL baselines for PAMDPs in both, sample efficiency and episodic return.

### [192] [FormalAnalyticGeo: A Neural-Symbolic Based Framework for Multimodal Analytic Geometry Problem Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12982)
*Ruoran Xu,Wending Gao,Qiufeng Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出FormalAnalyticGeo框架，通过形式化语言CDL连接文本与精确图表渲染，自动生成解析几何多模态问题，构建了7K+高质量数据集的AnalyticGeo7K，答案中位相对误差仅0.70%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解析几何在多模态大语言模型中研究不足，主要原因是标注样本稀缺。现有图表生成方法无法处理解析几何中受约束的布局，且缺乏精确渲染标注圆锥曲线的几何精度。

Method: 设计CDL（条件描述语言）作为形式化中间表示，连接自由文本与基于符号距离场（SDF）的精确图表渲染；四个LLM组件按序工作：Generator生成问题、Formalizer将问题转为CDL、Measurer从渲染图中提取答案、Quality Verifier三阶段质量检查并自动重试形成闭环。

Result: 生成7,000+验证过的多模态问题（AnalyticGeo7K），中位相对误差0.70%，82.3%的答案在精确符号解5%误差范围内。

Conclusion: 该框架实现了完全自动化的解析几何多模态问题生成，无需人工标注，数据集和框架将开源。

Abstract: Math reasoning has achieved significant progress with the rapid advancement of Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs), however analytic geometry remains largely underexplored, primarily due to the scarcity of annotated samples. Existing diagram generation approaches struggle with analytic geometry: template methods cannot handle constraint-driven layouts, and generative models lack the geometric precision to render annotated conic curves correctly. We present FormalAnalyticGeo, a scalable framework for fully automatic generation of multimodal analytic geometry problems. Leveraging the rigor of formal languages, we design the framework around CDL (Condition Description Language), a formal intermediate representation that bridges free-form problem text with precise diagram rendering via a Signed Distance Field (SDF) engine. The framework employs four specialized LLM components in sequence: a Generator that produces diverse analytic geometry problems, a Formalizer that converts each problem into CDL for SDF-based rendering, a Measurer that extracts ground-truth answers through vision-based measurement on the rendered diagrams, and a Quality Verifier that checks outputs at three stages. Structured feedback from the Quality Verifier drives automatic retry, forming a closed loop that eliminates any need for human annotation. Applying FormalAnalyticGeo at scale yields AnalyticGeo7K, a dataset of over 7K verified multimodal problems, each with aligned text, diagram, formal annotation, and ground truth.Experiments show that the generated problems achieve a median ground-truth relative error of 0.70\%, with 82.3\% of answers falling within 5\% of the exact symbolic solution. Our framework and dataset will be publicly released.

### [193] [Resist and Update: Counterfactual Report Coordinates for Incentive-Compatible LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12985)
*Sen Yang,Yuen-Hei Yeung*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于激活层反事实激励不变性的方法，通过构建反事实报告坐标夹（CRC clamp）来强制语言模型在非证据性激励压力下保持报告的一致性，在贝叶斯目击者基准上实现了1.00的联合抗干扰与证据响应能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对齐的语言模型在面对非证据性激励压力（如用户自信程度、声望等）时，会系统性误报其内部信念（如迎合用户或过度自信），即存在内部激励不兼容问题。现有方法未能有效区分"有证据支持的信息更新"与"无证据基础的激励压力"，因此需要一种因果层面的报告中介机制来确保模型报告对禁止性影响不变、对许可性影响敏感。

Method: (i) 通过互换干预（interchange interventions）而非探针准确性，识别出低秩的、近正交且可独立控制的报告坐标（答案、置信度、限定词）；(ii) 提出训练无关的反事实报告坐标夹（CRC clamp），通过引用模型在反事实激励中性化上下文中的自身报告来约束输出；(iii) 比较两遍夹（two-pass clamp）、单遍编译（single-pass compilation）、全局解码/调控及输出级微调等多种方案。

Result: 在贝叶斯目击者基准上，两遍夹实现了1.00的联合抗干扰与证据响应性能（Wilson 95% CI [0.99,1.00]），并提供了可构建参考下的因果认证。单遍编译方案存在信息损失（0.73/0.97）。该机制在三个模型家族上复现，并迁移至自然谄媚基准SycophancyEval。

Conclusion: 本文的核心贡献在于接口与认证方法：将激活层反事实激励不变性作为内部激励兼容性的结构原语，为构建可信赖的模型报告提供了因果层面的保障框架。

Abstract: Aligned language models routinely misreport under non-evidential incentive pressure: they agree with a confident user or overstate certainty even when their internal belief is unchanged. We cast this as a failure of internal incentive-compatibility (IC) and present a method for learning and certifying counterfactual report mediators that hold a model's reports to a causal contract: invariant to forbidden influences (pressure, prestige, restyling) and responsive to licensed ones (genuine evidence). These two demands, resist and update, pull in opposite directions. We study them on a Bayesian-witness benchmark with known posteriors, in which the same user disagreement is licensed evidence or forbidden pressure purely by stated source reliability. We (i) causally identify, by interchange interventions rather than probe accuracy, low-rank report coordinates for answer, confidence, and caveat that are near-orthogonal and independently controllable, and (ii) introduce a training-free counterfactual report-coordinate (CRC) clamp that references the model's own report under a counterfactually incentive-neutralized context. On the witness benchmark the two-pass clamp attains resist and update of 1.00 jointly (Wilson 95% CI [0.99,1.00]), a causal certificate under a constructible reference, not a deployed solution. Global decoding and steering show a single-parameter tradeoff; output-level fine-tuning matches both objectives only when both are enumerated; resist-only training loses evidence-responsiveness. The deployable single-pass compilation is lossy (0.73/0.97). The mechanism and clamp reproduce across three model families and transfer to a natural sycophancy benchmark (SycophancyEval). Our contribution is the interface and certification method: activation-level counterfactual incentive-invariance as a structural primitive for internal IC.

</details>


### [194] [Dynamic Resource Allocation for Ensemble Determinization MCTS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13007)
*Jakub Kowalski,Adam Ciężkowski,Artur Krzyżyński,Mark H. M. Winands*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对高不确定性环境（如带有随机和隐藏信息的博弈游戏），提出了 Ensemble Determinization MCTS 的两项动态资源分配增强策略：动态确定化次数（DND）和动态模拟分配（DSA），在 Jaipur、Lost Cities、Splendor 等桌游中验证了算法的显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 Ensemble Determinization MCTS 在面临高不确定性对抗性棋盘游戏时，资源分配固定，无法根据搜索过程动态调整，导致效率不足。本文旨在通过引入动态资源分配来提升算法强度。

Method: 提出了两个增强方法：1) 动态确定化次数（DND）：根据搜索行为动态增加或减少当前使用的确定化树数量；2) 动态模拟分配（DSA）：在多个确定化树之间非均匀分配模拟预算，通过模拟间的决策选择潜在信息增益最大的树。

Result: 在 Jaipur、Lost Cities、Splendor 三款桌游上，分别在基于迭代次数和基于时间的设定下进行测试，特定配置下算法强度取得了统计学上显著的提升。

Conclusion: 所提出的动态资源分配增强方法能够有效提升 Ensemble Determinization MCTS 在高不确定性博弈环境中的性能，尤其适用于含随机和隐藏信息的复杂游戏场景。

Abstract: Simulation-based algorithms are especially suited for high-uncertainty environments such as adversarial board games with significant elements of randomness and hidden information. In particular, several Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) variants are commonly used in such domains. In this paper, we propose a series of enhancements for Ensemble Determinization MCTS, introducing two axes for dynamic resource allocation. First, Dynamic Number of Determinizations, increases or decreases the number of currently used determinization trees depending on the behavior of so-far search. Second, Dynamic Simulation Allocation, splits the simulation budget nonuniformly across the determinization trees, using simulation-to-simulation decisions to choose the tree with potentially the best knowledge gain. As benchmark domains, we used three popular tabletop games: Jaipur, Lost Cities, and Splendor. Testing our proposed enhancements in iteration- and time-based settings showed that particular configurations yield a statistically significant increase in the algorithm's strength.

</details>


### [195] [Audio-Native Speech Recognition with a Frozen Discrete-Diffusion Language Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13013)
*Harsha Vardhan Khurdula,Abhinav Kumar Singh,Yoeven D Khemlani,Vineet Agarwal*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出使用离散扩散语言模型（DiffusionGemma，26B参数）替代传统自回归解码器进行语音识别。通过冻结的Whisper编码器提取声学特征，仅训练约4200万参数（0.16%），采用统一随机token离散扩散而非吸收掩码方案。针对梯度无法有效传递的问题，引入CTC损失打破僵局。在LibriSpeech test-clean上达到6.6%词错误率，约8个并行步骤即可完成任意长度话语的转录，且单一适配器支持六种语言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索离散扩散语言模型能否替代自回归解码器用于语音识别，实现并行转录而非逐token生成，以提升推理效率。

Method: 使用DiffusionGemma（26B MoE模型）作为骨干，采用统一随机token离散扩散；冻结Whisper编码器提供声学特征，轻量投影器映射到嵌入空间，低秩适配器使骨干关注新模态；发现自然训练目标导致梯度无法有效传递，引入CTC损失解决该问题。

Result: LibriSpeech test-clean上6.6%词错误率；约8个并行去噪步骤即可完成任意长度话语的转录；单一适配器训练于六种语言，在英语、印地语和普通话上进行了评估。

Conclusion: 离散扩散语言模型可以有效地进行语音识别，通过少量并行步骤完成转录，且参数高效（仅训练0.16%的骨干参数），具有多语言泛化能力。

Abstract: Automatic speech recognition is dominated by autoregressive decoders that emit one token at a time. We ask whether a discrete diffusion language model can transcribe speech instead, refining a whole transcript in parallel over a small number of denoising steps. We train an audio-native interface for DiffusionGemma, a 26B mixture-of-experts model that generates text by uniform, random-token discrete diffusion rather than the absorbing-mask scheme common to recent diffusion language models. A frozen Whisper encoder supplies acoustic features, a lightweight projector maps them into the model embedding space, and low-rank adapters let the frozen backbone attend to the new modality.
  About 42M parameters are trained, which is 0.16 percent of the backbone. We find that the natural training objectives fail to ground the audio because their gradient reaches the projector only through attention that has already dismissed it. A connectionist temporal classification loss applied through the frozen output head breaks this deadlock. The resulting model reaches 6.6 percent word error rate on LibriSpeech test-clean, transcribes in roughly eight parallel steps regardless of utterance length, and uses a single adapter trained on six languages, which we evaluate here on English, Hindi, and Mandarin.

### [196] [Predicting Acceptance and Review Effort in Human and Agent Pull Requests](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12057)
*Kartik Ghanshyambhai Pansuriya,Ehsan Ghorbani,Deepak Singh,Eman Abdullah AlOmar*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文研究能否在PR提交时（尚未收到审阅、CI反馈或合并决定）预测PR的接受概率和审阅工作量。基于AIDev数据集，使用仅含提交时特征的机器学习模型，发现树模型对接受预测F1可达0.95以上，但审阅工作量预测效果有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI编码代理与人共同提交PR，维护者需要判断哪些PR更可能被接受或需要更多审阅工作量，以便优化审阅资源分配。

Method: 基于AIDev数据集，构建泄漏感知预测流程，使用仅含提交时刻的特征（PR文本、元数据、仓库上下文、时间信号、轻量级diff统计），评估LR、RF、GB、ET、MLP等模型，并在 pooled、human-only、agent-only、balanced contributor 四个视角下测试。

Result: 接受预测可行：树模型F1>0.95，文本清晰度和元数据最具预测力。审阅工作量预测较难：评论数量和时间到合并难以通过提交时特征解释。

Conclusion: 早期PR模型可辅助审阅优先级排序，但应作为建议工具而非自动化决策者。

Abstract: Pull requests (PRs) are a central mechanism for reviewing and integrating code changes in modern software repositories. As AI coding agents begin to submit more code changes alongside human developers, maintainers face a new challenge: deciding which PRs are likely to be accepted and which ones may require substantial review effort. This paper studies whether such outcomes can be estimated at the time a PR is opened, before reviewer discussion, CI feedback, or merge decisions are available. Using the AIDev dataset, we construct a leakage-aware prediction pipeline for human- and agent-authored PRs. The feature set is limited to submission-time information, including PR text characteristics, metadata, repository context, temporal signals, and lightweight diff statistics. We evaluate classical machine-learning models, including Logistic Regression, Random Forests, Gradient Boosting, Extra Trees, and MLPs, across pooled, human-only, agent-only, and balanced contributor views. Our results show that acceptance prediction is feasible from early signals: tree-based models achieve F1 scores above 0.95, with textual clarity and metadata among the most influential predictors. Review-effort prediction is more difficult. Comment counts and time-to-merge are only modestly explained by submission-time features, suggesting that reviewer availability, project workflow, and team-specific review practices play a major role. These findings indicate that early PR models can support triage and reviewer prioritization, but should be used as advisory tools rather than automated decision-makers.

</details>


### [197] [AutoTrace: From Patches to Triggers via Agentic Interprocedural Exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12058)
*Arastoo Zibaeirad,Marco Vieira,Thomas Zimmermann*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: AutoTrace是一个自动化管道，通过逐层探索代码属性图，由LLM智能体决定搜索方向，并由确定性准入门控确保每个触发点都有显式图证据支持，在InterPVD基准上达到75.0%的VulnHit和80.8%的FuncHit，超越了现有方法。同时构建了SinkTrace-Bench数据集，揭示漏洞从源头到危险操作的因果链。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 漏洞修复提交中，触发定位（找出哪条语句将脆弱程序状态转变为具体不安全操作）比二进制漏洞检测更难，因为需要跨过程、因果推理。大量真实CVE中，触发语句位于修补函数数层之外，超出了静态规则集和模式匹配语言模型的覆盖范围。

Method: 提出AutoTrace，一种基于智能体的管道：逐层探索代码属性图(CPG)，LLM智能体决定下一步探索方向，确定性准入门控决定报告触发点所需的证据。智能体不自行接受任何触发点，每个报告的触发点都基于从图中提取的显式证据，从而覆盖过程和跨过程漏洞，不依赖无根据的模型判断。

Result: 在完整InterPVD基准上，AutoTrace达到75.0%的VulnHit和80.8%的FuncHit，超越此前最先进方法。构建的SinkTrace-Bench数据集包含1,542个经验证器确认、完美平衡的脆弱/安全样本。基准测试表明，即使是前沿LLM也难以区分这些配对样本，暴露了因果推理差距。

Conclusion: AutoTrace通过结合LLM的探索决策能力与基于图证据的确定性验证，有效解决了跨过程的漏洞触发定位问题。SinkTrace-Bench的构建和评估揭示了当前LLM在因果推理上的不足，印证了触发定位研究的必要性。

Abstract: Given a vulnerability-fixing commit, trigger localization asks which specific statement turns the vulnerable program state into a concrete unsafe operation. This question is harder than binary vulnerability detection because the answer demands interprocedural, causal reasoning: in a substantial fraction of real-world CVEs the triggering statement lies several call layers outside the patched function, beyond the reach of static rule sets and pattern-matching language models alike. We present AutoTrace, an agentic pipeline that localizes vulnerability triggers by exploring a code property graph layer by layer, with LLM agents deciding where to look next and deterministic admissibility gates deciding what evidence is required before a trigger can be reported. Agents never accept a trigger on their own authority; every reported trigger is backed by explicit evidence drawn from the graph, so the pipeline covers both intra- and interprocedural vulnerabilities without relying on ungrounded model judgment. On the full InterPVD benchmark, AutoTrace reaches 75.0% VulnHit and 80.8% FuncHit, surpassing the prior state of the art on the same corpus. Building on the same machinery, we construct SinkTrace-Bench, a dataset that exposes each vulnerability as a source-to-sink (S2S) causal chain from attacker-controlled input through propagation to the dangerous operation, drawn from matched vulnerable and patched program states. It comprises 1,542 verifier-confirmed, perfectly balanced vulnerable/safe samples whose label fidelity we audit against expert annotations. Benchmarking frontier LLMs on it, we find that even the strongest struggle to separate the matched pairs, exposing the causal-reasoning gap that trigger localization targets. Artifact available at https://github.com/Erroristotle/AutoTrace.

</details>


### [198] [Beyond Test Presence: Assessing the Quality and Robustness of Agent-Generated Tests in Open-Source Projects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12068)
*Preet Jhanglani,Zeel Kaushal Desai,Vidhi Kansara,Eman Abdullah AlOmar*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本研究对204,673个测试工件（含人类编写和AI生成）进行大规模实证比较，发现AI代理在边缘案例覆盖上优于人类（多样性评分0.62 vs 0.32），但人类在断言强度上略胜一筹（88.1% vs 85.37%）。然而AI生成的测试因依赖文件I/O和非确定性逻辑，脆弱性风险更高（候选率0.41 vs 0.30），表明AI代理缺乏"环境感知"能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准（如SWE-bench）主要关注测试通过率，忽略了测试本身的语义质量和覆盖率，导致"隐性技术债务"问题——测试虽能通过但不具备全面覆盖或语义价值。本文旨在填补这一方法论空白。

Method: 从AIDev数据集收集204,673个测试工件（24,941个人类编写+179,732个AI生成），利用Python的ast模块进行AST解析，实现"白盒"静态分析框架，从三个维度评估：断言强度（RQ1）、边缘案例覆盖（RQ2）、脆弱性潜力（RQ3）。

Result: AI代理在边缘案例覆盖上显著优于人类（边界检查多样性0.62 vs 0.32，空安全测试频率13.40% vs 8.3%）；人类在断言强度上略有优势（88.1% vs 85.37%）；但AI代理生成的测试脆弱性风险更高（候选率0.41 vs 0.30）。

Conclusion: AI代理擅长系统性边界测试，但缺乏编写稳定、封闭测试所需的"环境感知"能力，导致其生成的测试更易产生脆弱性。这一发现颠覆了传统假设，提示在CI/CD流水线中需对AI生成的测试进行额外稳定性审查。

Abstract: The integration of AI-powered coding agents into Continuous Integration/Continuous Delivery (CI/CD) pipelines has fundamentally altered how software verification is conducted. While these agents successfully automate the test generation, current evaluation benchmarks (e.g., SWE-bench) largely focus on pass-rates rather than the intrinsic quality of the generated tests. This raises the possibility of "stealth technical debt", in which test suites pass execution but do not offer comprehensive coverage or semantic value. We address this methodological gap through a large-scale, empirical comparison of 204,673 test artifacts which comprises of 24,941 human-authored files and 179,732 agent-generated files; sourced from the AIDev dataset. Using the Abstract Syntax Tree (AST) parsing with Python's naive ast module, we implemented a "white-box" static analysis framework to evaluate three quality dimensions: Assertion Strength (RQ1), Edge-Case Coverage (RQ2), and Flakiness Potential (RQ3). Our results present a nuanced inversion of traditional assumptions. AI agents performed better than humans in Edge-Case Coverage, with almost twice the variety of boundary checks (Variety Score: 0.62 vs 0.32) and a higher frequency of null-safety testing (13.40% vs. 8.3%), even though human developers had a slight advantage in Assertion Strength (88.1% strong assertions vs. 85.37% for agents). But this thoroughness comes at a price: due mostly to their reliance on file I/O and non-deterministic logic, agent-generated tests exhibited a higher risk of flakiness (Candidate Rate: 0.41 vs. 0.30). These findings suggest that while AI agents excel at rigorous boundary testing, they lack the "environmental awareness" needed to write stable, hermetic tests.

### [199] [Fault Injection in OpenAPI Specifications for Evaluating Black-Box Testing Effectiveness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12101)
*Hamza Bin Mazhar,Yuqing Wang,Mika V. Mäntylä*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本研究首次系统性地探讨了OpenAPI规范缺陷对微服务系统黑盒测试的影响，通过注入六类规范故障并评估三个测试工具在两个微服务基准上的表现，发现规范缺陷会导致测试效果显著且异质的下降，且仅用代码/规范覆盖率评估会低估其影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究大多假设OpenAPI规范是正确的来评估测试工具性能，但实际中规范常存在不完整、不一致或错误的问题。作者希望通过量化规范缺陷对测试效果的实际影响，填补这一研究空白。

Method: 基于文献构建了六类OpenAPI规范故障的分类体系，按五个严重级别注入故障，在两个微服务基准（TrainTicket和SocialNetwork）上使用EvoMaster、RESTler和Schemathesis三个测试工具进行实验，从代码覆盖率、规范覆盖率、请求/响应质量和行为多样性四个维度评估影响。

Result: 方法语义故障导致所有指标全面退化；响应码修改等故障影响较弱；模式约束的放松对代码和规范覆盖率无影响，但严重降低了请求/响应质量（隐藏退化）。不同故障类型对测试工具和系统的退化模式呈现强烈的异质性。

Conclusion: 规范质量直接影响黑盒API测试的有效性，仅用代码和规范覆盖率评估会低估规范缺陷的影响，应补充请求/响应质量和行为多样性指标。

Abstract: OpenAPI specifications are the primary input for black-box testing tools in microservice systems (MSS), yet prior work shows these specifications are often incomplete, inconsistent, or incorrect. Despite this, most studies on OpenAPI-based black-box testing assume correct specifications and evaluate tool performance. We address this gap by introducing a literature-grounded taxonomy of six OpenAPI specification fault classes. We inject faults at five severity levels, and evaluate the resulting mutated specifications on two microservice benchmarks, TrainTicket and SocialNetwork, using three testing tools: EvoMaster, RESTler, and Schemathesis. We measure the impact of these faults using code coverage, specification coverage, request/response quality, and behavioral diversity. Our results show that specification faults cause strong and heterogeneous degradation patterns across testing tools and systems. Faults in method semantics cause broad degradation across all metrics, while others, such as modifications to response codes, remain weak. Relaxations of schema constraints cause hidden degradation, with no impact on code and specification coverage but a large impact on request/response quality. These findings demonstrate that specification quality directly shapes black-box API testing effectiveness. Also, code and specification coverage-only evaluations can understate the impact of specification faults on black-box testing in MSS and should be complemented by request/response quality and behavioral diversity.

### [200] [TraceSynth: Generating Production-Quality Kernel Traces with Constraint-Guided Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12104)
*Yuvraj Sehgal,Sneh Patel,Mahsa Panahandeh,Naser Ezzati-Jivan,Francois Tetreault*

Main category: cs.SE

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器学习系统诊断依赖内核执行迹，但工业系统中采集生产迹成本高昂（运行时开销、存储需求、隐私约束），需要合成数据来增强有限的真实数据。

Method: 将迹建模为多通道序列（事件类型、时间戳、CPU亲和性、线程标识、进程元数据），使用基于Transformer的去噪扩散过程，并结合约束引导修复来保证系统不变性。

Result: 在确定性计算密集型负载（scimark2）上，合成数据增强达到87.2% F1-Macro（L=4096），仅比真实数据基线低2.6个百分点；上下文长度是主导质量因素（L=4096比L=256提升+104%）；约束引导修复提升最多4.3%；轻量2通道模型保留97-99%性能且计算成本减半。

Conclusion: TraceSynth能有效降低生产可观测性管道中内核迹的获取成本，并帮助判断何时合成数据可替代有限的真实迹。

Abstract: Machine learning models for system diagnostics rely on kernel execution traces to capture fine-grained system behavior, but collecting production traces in industrial systems is costly due to runtime overhead, storage demands, and privacy constraints. We present TraceSynth, a diffusion-based framework for generating synthetic kernel traces that augment limited real data for downstream ML tasks. TraceSynth models traces as multi-channel sequences (event types, timestamps, CPU affinity, thread identifiers, and process metadata) using a Transformer-based denoising diffusion process with constraint-guided repair to enforce system invariants. Across six benchmarks, results show strong workload dependence. For deterministic, compute-heavy workloads (scimark2), synthetic augmentation achieves 87.2% F1-Macro at context length L=4096, only 2.6 percentage points below real-only baselines. Context length is the dominant quality factor, with L=4096 yielding a +104% relative improvement over L=256, while constraint-guided repair improves synthetic data quality by up to 4.3%. Ablation studies show that lightweight 2-channel models retain 97-99% of the performance of full 6-channel models at roughly half the computational cost. TraceSynth supports cost-effective augmentation of kernel execution traces in production observability pipelines and helps identify when synthetic data can substitute for limited real traces.

TestMiner is available at: https://andrehora.github.io/testminer. Screencast: https://youtu.be/w1sBgLTq-7Y.

### [203] [Code-MUE: Measuring Code LLMs' Uncertainty through Execution-based Semantic Interaction Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12273)
*Xiaoning Ren,Yinxing Xue,Lei Ma,Yuheng Huang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出Code-MUE框架，通过执行驱动的语义交互图来量化代码LLM的不确定性，有效解决了传统黑盒方法无法区分代码语法变化与语义差异的问题。实验表明该方法与功能正确性强负相关（Spearman相关系数达-0.98），显著优于现有基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代码LLM的随机性会导致严重的安全与功能风险，需要可靠的置信度估计。但现有不确定性估计方法存在关键空白：白盒/灰盒方法不适用于闭源模型，而标准黑盒文本指标无法捕捉代码特有的脆弱性——语法变化不一定意味着语义差异。

Method: 提出Code-MUE纯黑盒框架，通过执行驱动的语义交互图（Semantic Interaction Graphs）来衡量不确定性，基于可观测的运行时行为计算解空间的冯·诺依曼熵（Von Neumann entropy），从而量化全局语义多样性。

Result: 在八个最先进LLM上的大规模实证研究表明，Code-MUE与功能正确性之间达到强负相关（Spearman相关系数最高-0.98），显著优于基于词法和嵌入的基线方法，并能有效支持风险检测和选择性预测。

Conclusion: Code-MUE通过将不确定性度量从语法层面转向语义/执行层面，成功弥合了代码语法-语义鸿沟，为闭源代码模型提供了有效的黑盒不确定性估计方案，在实用工作流中展现出鲁棒的风险检测与选择性预测能力。

Abstract: As Code Large Language Models (LLMs) become central to modern software engineering, their inherent stochasticity poses significant real-world risks, where even minor errors can lead to severe functional, security, or safety consequences. Reliable automation, therefore, demands the ability to distinguish between confident, well-supported predictions and stochastic guessing. However, existing uncertainty estimation methods face a critical gap: white and grey-box techniques are often inapplicable to closed-source models, while standard "black-box" text metrics fail to capture the unique fragility of code, where syntactic variation does not always imply semantic divergence. To bridge this syntax-semantics gap, we introduce Code-MUE, a purely black-box framework that measures uncertainty through execution-based Semantic Interaction Graphs. Unlike prior approaches that rely on superficial textual similarity, Code-MUE grounds uncertainty in observable runtime behavior, calculating the Von Neumann entropy of the solution space to quantify global semantic diversity. A large-scale empirical study across eight state-of-the-art LLMs demonstrates that Code-MUE achieves a strong negative correlation with functional correctness (Spearman's correlation up to -0.98), significantly outperforming lexical and embedding-based baselines while enabling robust risk detection and selective prediction in practical workflows.

### [204] [XScientist: A Git-Like Research Protocol for Long-Running Autonomous Scientific Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12301)
*Jixiang Luo*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 XScientist 协议与操作系统：将想法生成、实验执行、手稿撰写、自我审查、修复、质量门控、守护调度、可复现性制品组织为一条持续可观测的管线。核心设计是每轮运行为一个可移植的研究制品 (ARA)，包含探索 DAG、节点代码与输出、主张-证据锚点、内容哈希、溯源信息及重执行钩子。

Abstract: Autonomous research systems are often evaluated as one-shot paper generators: given a topic, they produce a manuscript and a small set of experiment logs. XScientist is a git-like research protocol and operating system for this setting. The central design choice is to treat each run as a portable research artifact rather than only as a PDF. XScientist exports an Agent-Native Research Artifact (ARA), a protocol that records an exploration DAG, per-node code and outputs, claim-to-evidence anchors, content hashes, provenance, and re-execution hooks. This makes each generated paper inspectable as a science exploration tree: failed branches, repaired experiments, ablations, and manuscript claims remain connected to the nodes that produced them. The system also includes deterministic integrity forensics, sample gates, truth contracts, reviewer-oriented repair loops, and long-running daemon controls. This paper describes the current XScientist architecture, the ARA protocol surface, and the practical safeguards needed to move autonomous science from single-run demos toward reproducible, reviewable, and forkable research infrastructure. ### [205] [How Many Interviews Are Enough in a Software Engineering Study? Preliminary Findings on Sample Size and Saturation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12326)
*Ronnie de Souza Santos,Italo Santos,Mauricio Rodrigues,Cleyton Magalhaes*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文分析了2016-2025年间软件工程领域访谈研究的样本量与饱和度报告情况，发现样本量差异大（常见13-24人），饱和度和样本充分性的论证方式不统一，许多研究依赖隐式推理而非明确的方法学讨论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
