Method: 分析了2016-2025年间发表在主要软件工程会议/期刊上的论文，重点关注访谈样本量、饱和度讨论和样本充分性论证。

Result: 样本量差异大：小样本（<12人）常见于专业工业背景，最常规模拟为13-24人；饱和度和样本充分性论证方式不统一，多依赖隐式或上下文推理。

Conclusion: 为访谈类软件工程研究的方法学报告实践提供了初步实证洞察，并促进了关于定性研究严谨性和透明度的持续讨论。

Abstract: Background. Interview based studies are widely used in empirical software engineering to investigate human, organizational, and socio technical phenomena, yet interview sample adequacy and saturation are reported inconsistently across the literature. Aims. This paper investigates how interview sample adequacy and saturation are operationalized in empirical software engineering research. Method. We analyzed papers published between 2016 and 2025 across major software engineering venues, focusing on interview sample sizes, saturation discussions, and sample adequacy justifications. Results. Preliminary findings indicate substantial variation in sample sizes, from highly specialized small sample studies to broader investigations involving large interview datasets. Studies involving fewer than 12 interviewees were common and frequently associated with specialized industrial contexts or constrained organizational access. However, the most recurrent range was 13 to 24 interviewees, suggesting that moderate sized samples represent the most common configuration in empirical software engineering research. Saturation and sample adequacy justification were heterogeneous, with many studies relying on implicit or contextual reasoning rather than explicit methodological discussion. Conclusions. Our findings provide initial empirical insights into methodological reporting practices in interview based software engineering research and contribute to ongoing discussions regarding qualitative rigor and transparency.

### [206] [Skills That Don't Exist: A Large-Scale Study of Hallucinated Skill Recommendation in LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12340)
*Weifeng Yuan,Wenbo Guo,Feng Dong,Haoyu Wang,Yang Liu*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文揭示了LLM代理在推荐和安装技能时会凭空编造不存在的技能名称（技能名称幻觉），攻击者可利用此漏洞预注册恶意技能实施供应链攻击。大规模测量发现所有模型均存在该问题，幻觉率平均36%以上，且生成的假名具有高度一致性。现有防御措施在安全性与可用性之间存在严重冲突，需要生态层面的结构性修复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM代理可以从开放注册中心下载技能，但代理会编造不存在的技能名称，这为供应链攻击提供了入口。攻击者可收集这些假名并预先注册恶意技能，等待受害者安装。作者旨在首次大规模测量这一漏洞的严重性。

Method: 对15,000条提示在12种配置（4个独立LLM和8个代理）下进行系统评估，将不在任何活跃注册中心和GitHub中的名称保守计为幻觉。同时测试了4种模型级防御措施的效果。

Result: 所有配置均存在幻觉，独立LLM平均幻觉率36.0%，代理平均36.9%，真实开发者问题场景下高达43.1%。共产生5,669个独特幻觉名称，且这些名称在不同提示和模型间高度重复。最强防御（检索接地）虽将幻觉率从40.8%降至3.2%，但正确推荐率仅为六分之一。

Conclusion: 技能名称幻觉是一个极易利用的安全漏洞，对攻击者而言成本极低。仅靠提示工程或模型调优无法修复，需要生态层面的结构性变革，包括注册中心名称预留和经过验证的推荐管道。

Abstract: LLM agents acquire new capabilities by downloading skills from open registries. Instead of browsing these catalogs manually, developers typically ask the agent to recommend and install a skill. This convenience hides a risk: agents frequently invent names for skills that exist in no registry. We term this flaw skill name hallucination. A fake name may seem harmless, but it opens the door to supply-chain attacks. Because registries rarely verify publishers, an adversary can prompt the agent, collect the fake names it returns, pre-register malicious skills under them, and wait for a victim to install the payload. We conducted the first large-scale measurement of skill name hallucination, evaluating 15,000 prompts across 12 configurations (4 standalone LLMs and 8 agents). We conservatively counted a name as hallucinated only if it was missing from all live registries and GitHub. The results reveal a systemic vulnerability: every configuration hallucinates. Rates average 36.0% for standalone LLMs and 36.9% for agents, rising to 43.1% on real-world developer questions. In total, the systems generated 5,669 distinct hallucinated names. Crucially, these names are not random noise. Agents repeat the same fake names across prompts and models, giving attackers highly reliable targets to hijack. Finally, we tested four model-level defenses and found a severe conflict between security and usability. The strongest, retrieval grounding, cut the hallucination rate from 40.8% to 3.2% but crippled usefulness: even the best-defended system recommended the correct skill only about one in six times. Skill name hallucination is thus a highly exploitable vulnerability requiring minimal attacker effort. Fixing it cannot rely on prompt engineering or model tuning alone. It demands ecosystem-wide structural changes: registry-level name reservations and verified recommendation pipelines.

</details>


### [207] [Detecting Rendering Bugs in Imperative Data Visualization Libraries via Equivalent Mutations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12363)
*Weiqi Lu,Yongqiang Tian*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: VIZDETOUR通过等价变异自动检测命令式数据可视化库的渲染错误，发现47个新bug。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 命令式可视化库的渲染错误难以自动检测，因为缺乏预期输出的oracle，且图形元素间的更新可能产生微妙不一致。

Method: 将oracle问题转化为等价检测问题：在种子绘图脚本后追加语义等价的API调用序列（先修改状态再恢复），通过感知哈希比较渲染输出是否一致。

Result: 在matplotlib、bokeh、plotly上发现47个未知bug，39个已确认，18个已修复。

Conclusion: 等价变异是一种有效的渲染bug检测策略，能够发现真实库中的未知错误。

Abstract: Imperative data visualization libraries construct plots through a sequence of stateful API calls that incrementally create and update graphic elements. Rendering bugs in these libraries often manifest as incorrect visual outputs rather than crashes or exceptions, making them difficult to detect automatically. A fundamental challenge is the lack of an oracle that specifies the expected rendering of an arbitrary plotting script. Furthermore, an update to one graphic element may inadvertently affect other elements or properties, leading to subtle inconsistencies in the final rendered image.
  This paper presents VIZDETOUR, an automated testing approach for detecting rendering bugs in imperative data visualization libraries via equivalent mutations. The key idea is to transform the oracle problem into an equivalence-checking problem. Starting from a seed plotting script, VIZDETOUR appends a short sequence of semantically equivalent API calls that temporarily modify the visualization state and then restore it to its original state. Although these mutations exercise different execution paths, they should preserve the final rendering. Any visual discrepancy between the original and mutated scripts therefore indicates a rendering bug. To generate such mutations, VIZDETOUR constructs a render tree from the seed script, identifies traceable graphic elements and mutable properties, and synthesizes endpoint-preserving mutation sequences. It then compares the rendered outputs using perceptual hashing. We evaluate VIZDETOUR on matplotlib, bokeh, and plotly using scripts collected from their official example galleries. VIZDETOUR discovers 47 previously unknown bugs, of which 39 are confirmed and 18 are fixed.

</details>

Result: 实验结果表明，EVITA比现有方法触发了更多样化的AV交互行为，从而提高了发现安全关键行为的可能性。

Common scenario-based testing approaches set the environment and the surrounding traffic and test a single AV. Recent studies show that the approaches that test single AVs miss critical behaviors that emerge from interactions among multiple AVs. Effective approaches to test scenarios that emerge from n-way interactions must address the combinatorial explosion that the presence of multiple AVs further exacerbates. In this paper, we propose EVITA, an approach that leverages multi-objective optimization to generate scenarios that trigger multiple and diverse AVs interactions, while minimizing the complexity of the generated scenarios, to effectively test multiple interacting AVs and reveal safety-critical scenarios that current approaches overlook. The experimental results that we discuss in this paper confirm that EVITA triggers a higher variety of AVs interactions than state-of-the-art approaches, thus improving the likelihood to reveal safety-critical behaviors.

Although large language models (LLMs) show promising performance for MNP, two challenges remain. First, existing evaluations mainly rely on token similarity metrics, which often fail to reflect human judgments of semantic quality. Second, current LLM-based MNP methods usually generate names through direct code-to-name mapping, which differs from the human process of understanding functionality before naming. To address these challenges, we conduct empirical studies on LLM-based evaluation and MNP strategies. We compare 6 metric-based evaluators, 5 LLM-based evaluators, and 6 human evaluators. Results show that LLM-based evaluators, especially DeepSeek-based evaluators, are more consistent with human judgments than traditional metrics. We further compare direct generation and summarization-and-refinement strategies. Results indicate that summarization and refinement generally improve the semantic quality of generated names. Case studies reveal three limitations: inaccurate summaries, semantic misalignment, and close semantic scores. Based on these findings, we propose SMNP, an MNP approach combining MNP-oriented summarization and chain-of-thought enhanced refinement. ### [211] [Agent-Safety Evaluations as Load-Bearing Evidence: A Vendor-Neutral, Cross-Harness Reconstructability Metric](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12469)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI安全评价结果缺乏负载支撑力——相同的表面结果（如任务成功、攻击成功、监控分数）可能建立在截然不同的证据基础之上，缺乏厂商中立、可运行的工具来评估证据能否重构决策所依赖的结论。

Result: 在公开和捆绑轨迹上（无需新模型运行），十二字段充分性在四个共享表面解读的输入上跨度为0.458-0.833；所有打分轨迹中重放前置条件均未满足。在合成发布-门控对上，充分性门控阻挡了原始变体（0.542）而通过了仪器化变体（0.667）。

Conclusion: 安全评价声明应附带其可复现性向量；本文提供完整可复现包以再生每个报告数值。

Abstract: Many agent-safety evaluation results are not yet load-bearing evidence: identical nominal outcomes (task success, attack success, monitor scores) may sit atop materially different evidence regimes. No vendor-neutral, runnable instrument scores reconstructability as an evaluation-validity metric: whether captured evidence can reconstruct the decision a claim depends on. This paper introduces a property-level reconstructability metric over eight decision-property classes and a cross-harness adapter emitting per-decision Evidence Sufficiency Cards backing a per-run monitor-coverage release check. It specifies a counterfactual-replay intervention protocol, implements its replayability-precondition probe, and defines a claim-evidence overclaim gap. On public and bundled traces, without new model runs, twelve-field sufficiency spans 0.458-0.833 across four inputs sharing a surface reading; replay preconditions are unmet in every scored trace. In a synthetic release-gate pair, the sufficiency gate blocks the raw variant (0.542) and passes the instrumented (0.667). Safety-evaluation claims should travel with their reconstructability vector; a reproducibility package regenerates every reported number.

### [212] [Taming the Drift: Context-aware Repair of Dockerfile Drift during Software Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12541)
*Chengjie Wang,Jingzheng Wu,Xiang Ling,Tianyue Luo,Chen Zhao*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: Cadre是一个上下文感知的Dockerfile漂移自动修复框架，通过构建上下文依赖图(CDG)和两步工作流，在1040个真实漂移实例上达到35.22%的修复率，比基于规则的方法提升2.78倍，比最佳LLM基线提升1.24倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Dockerfile与其演进中的源代码之间会发生漂移（drift），导致CI/CD构建失败。现有基于规则和检索的修复方法孤立分析Dockerfile，难以处理依赖上下文的失败场景。

Method: 提出Cadre框架：1) 静态分析构建上下文感知依赖图(CDG)，映射每条Dockerfile指令到文件级和指令间依赖；2) 根据CDG选择因果相关的上下文；3) 从上下文中生成针对性补丁。同时提出DodeX流水线，从GitHub Actions CI日志挖掘真实漂移实例，构建包含原始CI参数的D³基准数据集。

Result: 在D³基准（1040个漂移实例）上，Cadre修复率达35.22%，是规则基线的2.78倍，最佳LLM基线的1.24倍。95.25%的提示保持在30k token以下，避免了其他LLM方法的提示溢出失败。消融实验验证了CDG和两步工作流的有效性。随着漂移跨提交老化，Cadre相对于仅diff方法优势持续增加。

Conclusion: 显式依赖建模对上下文感知的基础设施即代码维护至关重要。Cadre通过构建依赖图实现精确上下文选择，有效提升了Dockerfile漂移的自动修复能力。代码和数据已开源。

Abstract: Docker is widely used to create reproducible build environments, but Dockerfile drift, the divergence between a Dockerfile and its evolving source code, can cause CI/CD builds to fail. Existing rule-based and retrieval-based repair approaches analyze Dockerfiles in isolation and therefore struggle with context-dependent failures. We present Cadre, a context-aware framework for automated Dockerfile drift repair. Cadre uses static analysis to construct a Context-aware Dependency Graph (CDG), which maps each Dockerfile instruction to its file-level and inter-instruction dependencies. Guided by the CDG, Cadre first selects the context causally relevant to a failure and then generates a targeted patch from that context. We also introduce DodeX, a pipeline that mines real-world Dockerfile drift instances from GitHub Actions CI logs while preserving the complete build configurations omitted by static-snapshot datasets. Using DodeX, we construct $D^3$, a benchmark of 1,040 drift instances reproducible locally with the original CI parameters. Across $D^3$, Cadre achieves a 35.22\% repair rate, 2.78$\times$ that of the rule-based baseline and 1.24$\times$ that of the best LLM-based baseline. Its two-step workflow keeps 95.25\% of prompts below 30k tokens and avoids the prompt-overflow failures that prevent competing LLM-based methods from producing patches in 41 to 58 cases per method. Ablation results confirm that both the CDG and the two-step workflow improve repair performance. Cadre's advantage over diff-only approaches also increases as drift ages across commits, supporting explicit dependency modeling for context-aware infrastructure-as-code maintenance. Code and data are available at https://github.com/dw763j/Cadre.

</details>


### [213] [Evaluation Bias and Epistemic Inequality in Global Software Development](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12563)
*Sam Khosravi,Amir H. Payberah*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过混合方法研究比较了东非（卢旺达、乌干达）和西北欧（瑞典、荷兰）48名软件工程师的表现，发现尽管卢旺达高级工程师的实际表现与欧洲同行相当，但欧洲参与者系统性低估了东非工程师的能力，揭示了全球软件开发中评估能力的公平性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 全球软件开发中存在基于区域背景的能力评估偏见，需要关注公平性和问责机制；不同地区的工作方式各具特色且具有互补性，不应以单一标准评判。

Despite the rapid growth of African technology ecosystems, empirical evidence on everyday engineering practice and evaluation in these contexts remains limited. We present findings from an on-site mixed-methods study with 48 software engineers across four countries. The study combines programming, system design, and code review tasks with semi-structured interviews. Our results reveal consistent gaps between measured performance and perceived competence. Senior engineers in Rwanda often performed at a level comparable to that of their European peers, yet European participants systematically underestimated the competence of East African engineers. ### [214] [Hierarchical Fault Localization for Autonomous Driving Systems with Hypothesis Validation and Intent Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12598)
*Rui Zheng,Changwen Li,Yi Ji,Rongjie Yan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: HINT是一个两阶段框架，通过假设验证和意图分析实现ADS分层故障定位，先因果推理定位模块，再通过可靠性感知一致性检查定位可疑代码，在Apollo上达到77.8%的端到端Class@5准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ADS测试技术可检测系统级故障或归因到粗粒度模块，但无法定位源代码根因，调试仍需开发者手动关联行为违规与复杂实现逻辑，工作量大。

Method: 两阶段框架：Phase I将触发失败的执行记录转化为多模态抽象，通过因果推理定位责任模块；Phase II重建设计意图和实现行为，通过可靠性感知一致性检查定位可疑代码，无需昂贵的重仿真。

Result: 在Apollo系统上针对多种故障模式和模块进行评估，在模块级诊断和代码级定位指标上均取得最强整体性能，对真实bug的端到端Class@5准确率达77.8%。

Conclusion: HINT有效填补了ADS故障定位从粗粒度模块到细粒度源代码之间的空白，通过多模态抽象与意图分析实现了高效、准确的分层根因定位。

Abstract: Comprehensive testing is essential for the safety and reliability of Autonomous Driving Systems (ADS). Existing techniques can detect system-level failures or attribute them to coarse-grained modules, but they often fall short of localizing the root cause in source code. As a result, debugging remains labor-intensive, requiring developers to connect behavioral violations with complex implementation logic. To address this gap, we present HINT, a two-phase framework for hierarchical ADS fault localization based on hypothesis validation and intent analysis. In Phase I, HINT transforms failure-triggering execution recordings into multi-modal abstractions and uses causal reasoning to identify the responsible module. In Phase II, it reconstructs design-side intent and implementation-side behavior, then localizes suspicious code through reliability-aware consistency checking, without costly re-simulation. We evaluate HINT on Apollo across diverse failure modes and modules. The results show that HINT achieves the strongest overall performance across module-level diagnosis and code-level localization metrics, with 77.8% end-to-end Class@5 accuracy on real-world bugs.

### [215] [Multi-Perspective Agentic Program Repair via Code Property Graphs and Temporal Execution Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12605)
*Zhili Huang,Ling Xu,Hongyu Zhang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: CT-Repair是一个智能APR框架，通过代码属性图(CPG)和时间执行图(TEG)表示静态和动态证据，采用三阶段过滤流水线压缩TEG，并利用三个有限状态机引导的代理从静态、动态和混合角度分析错误，生成基于证据的修复策略。在Defects4J v3.0的854个Java错误上，混合配置正确修复489个，GPT-5.4-mini配置修复388个，比ReinFix和RepairAgent分别多19和30个。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM辅助自动程序修复存在两个局限：原始执行轨迹过大且重复，不适合作为模型上下文；重复的补丁采样可能产生不同实现但未产生不同的根本原因假设或修复策略。

Method: CT-Repair框架将静态和动态证据表示为可查询的代码属性图(CPG)和时间执行图(TEG)，通过三阶段过滤流水线构建紧凑TEG，三个有限状态机引导的代理分别从静态、动态和混合视角分析错误并生成修复策略，最后通过策略引导生成候选补丁并利用验证反馈优化最佳策略。

Result: 在Defects4J v3.0的854个Java错误上，混合配置修复489个；GPT-5.4-mini配置修复388个，超越ReinFix(369)和RepairAgent(358)；三种证据视角的联合比最强单一视角多修复99个；执行过滤将候选方法范围缩小94.85%，行为过滤进一步减少55.97%的运行记录。

Conclusion: 结构化的运行时证据和多视角推理可以在不依赖更大补丁生成预算的情况下提高修复效果。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have improved automated program repair (APR), but two limitations remain. First, raw execution traces are often too large and repetitive to serve as effective model context. Second, repeated patch sampling may produce different implementations without yielding distinct root-cause hypotheses or repair strategies. We present CT-Repair, an agentic APR framework representing static and dynamic evidence as queryable Code Property Graph (CPG) and Temporal Execution Graph (TEG). CT-Repair applies a three-stage filtering pipeline to construct compact TEGs. Three finite-state-machine-guided agents analyze each bug from static, dynamic, and hybrid perspectives and independently produce evidence-grounded repair strategies. A strategy-guided generation procedure instantiates these strategies as candidate patches and uses validation feedback to refine the most promising strategy.
  We evaluate CT-Repair on 854 Java bugs from Defects4J v3.0. In the mixed-model configuration, CT-Repair correctly repairs 489 bugs. Under a controlled GPT-5.4-mini configuration, it repairs 388 bugs, 19 and 30 more than ReinFix and RepairAgent, respectively. The union of the three evidence perspectives repairs 99 more bugs than the strongest individual perspective. The filtering pipeline also compacts runtime evidence, with execution filtering narrowing the candidate method scope by 94.85% on average and behavior filtering further reducing retained runtime records by 55.97%. These results show that structured runtime evidence and multi-perspective reasoning can improve repair effectiveness without relying solely on a larger patch-generation budget.

</details>


### [216] [Line-Anchored Feedback Cuts Token Costs and Improves Correctness in AI Code Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12713)
*William Franz Lamberti*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结构化、行锚定的反馈方式（FileMark），相比整体式提示，可显著降低生成式AI代码编辑中的token消耗（最高降低58%），同时提升正确性，尤其对100行以上的大文件和较弱模型效果更明显。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式AI代码编辑中，生成的token数量直接决定成本、延迟和能耗。现有整体式提示（holistic prompt）效率低下，需要探索更高效的反馈格式来降低这些开销。

Method: 提出FileMark——一个VSCodium扩展，支持对任何文件进行结构化、行锚定的内联注释。通过与整体式提示（对照组）进行配对实验对比，评估token节省和正确性表现。同时进行了探索性实验，由工具而非AI模型直接应用编辑补丁。

Result: 行锚定方法使token生成量降低22%（Claude Opus）到58%（Claude Sonnet），100行以上文件降低达24%-80%。7个模型中有4个在多重检验校正后仍显著减少token。正确性方面，整体提升2.0分，3个本地模型提升5-7分。在探索性实验中，100行以上文件的本地模型正确性近乎翻三倍。

Conclusion: 行锚定反馈能减少强模型的token开销，同时提升弱模型的正确性。将编辑应用负担从模型转移到工具端，能进一步放大正确性收益。

Abstract: Generated tokens are a direct driver of the cost, latency, and energy of generative AI (GAI) code editing. We show the format of feedback is a lever on all three. We compare two deliveries of the same requested changes: a holistic prompt (control) versus the structured, line-anchored export of FileMark (treatment). FileMark is a VSCodium extension for inline comments on any file. In a paired experiment line anchoring cut generated tokens by 22% (Claude Opus) and 58% (Claude Sonnet), reaching 24%-80% on files of 100 lines or more, with four of seven models generating significantly fewer tokens after multiple-testing correction. Correctness rose where models had headroom: +2.0 points pooled and +5 to +7 points for three of five local models. An exploratory experiment in which the harness, not the GAI model, applies function-level patches shows the correctness benefit grows further when the edit-application burden is lifted: local-model correctness on 100+ line files roughly triples under anchoring. Line-anchored feedback reduces what stronger models spend and improves what weaker models get right.

</details>


### [217] [Toward Localizing and Repairing Bias in Transformer Attention Heads](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12863)
*Sigma Jahan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出ROBIN方法，通过识别和修改注意力头来减少语言模型中的性别偏见，在保持语言质量的同时降低了WinoBias差距。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出ROBIN方法，一种白盒注意力头级公平性调试方法。该方法利用对公平性探针的敏感性对注意力头进行排序，然后从选定的头输出中移除小的偏见子空间。

Result: 在四个模型的初步研究中，ROBIN方法在所有模型上均降低了WinoBias差距，且比完全置零注意力头的方法更好地保持了语言建模质量。

Existing fairness testing and repair methods largely operate at the input-output or retraining level, while recent work suggests that bias-related behavior can concentrate in a small set of attention heads. This paper studies whether attention heads can be localized and repaired through a targeted inference-time intervention. We introduce ROBIN, a white-box head-level fairness debugging method that ranks attention heads using sensitivity to fairness probes and removes a small bias subspace from selected head outputs. In a four-model pilot study, ROBIN reduces the measured WinoBias gap across all models while preserving language-modeling quality better than whole-head zeroing. These preliminary results suggest that head-level bias repair should consider not only which heads are selected, but also how selected heads are modified.

*Sigma Jahan*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度学习系统常因细微的实现故障而失败，但软件工程社区缺乏公开的、带故障记录和特征提取的逐轮训练数据集，无法有效支持故障检测与诊断研究。

Method: 从Stack Overflow收集59个TensorFlow/Keras DNN程序，应用27种源代码变换引入7类已知故障，生成9,845次故障运行和4,382次正常运行，记录每轮训练的26维特征（权重、梯度、激活值、准确率、损失趋势、学习率、硬件使用等）和4项评估指标。

Abstract: Deep learning systems often fail due to subtle implementation faults that alter training behavior. Recent work has studied how to detect and diagnose such failures from changes observed across training epochs. However, the software engineering community still lacks a public dataset of per-epoch training runs with documented fault history, feature extraction details, and clear reuse support for fault detection and diagnosis tasks. We present Deep4ge, a controlled benchmark of 14,227 training runs generated from 59 adapted TensorFlow/Keras deep neural network (DNN) programs collected from Stack Overflow. We generated faulty variants using 27 source-code transformations that introduce known faults across seven categories. The dataset contains 9,845 faulty runs and 4,382 correct baseline runs. For each run, we record 4 evaluation metrics and 26 features that measure training behavior at every epoch. These features capture weights, gradients, activations, accuracy and loss trends, learning rate, and hardware use. Deep4ge supports binary fault detection, multi-class fault diagnosis, and early fault prediction from partial training runs. We release the dataset and fault-injection framework at https://doi.org/10.5281/zenodo.20337241.

### [220] [Form, Not Content? A Preregistered, Placebo-Controlled Evaluation of Learned Error-Conditioned Self-Repair Through Prompts and Weights in Frozen Small Code Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12962)
*Mehmet Iscan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出PoPE（波普尔安慰剂对照评估）方法，用于量化LLM生成的代码在失败后能否利用错误信息进行修复。在0.5-1.5B的小型代码模型上，通过提示通道和权重通道进行实验，结果显示错误内容并未显著提升修复成功率，表明模型并未真正"理解"错误信息，而是将其内化为条件性信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码LLM自我修复研究缺乏安慰剂对照实验，无法区分错误信息的真正利用与虚假关联。作者将失败程序视为猜想（conjecture），将执行反例视为相对于oracle的证伪（refutation），希望建立严谨的因果测量标准。

Method: 提出PoPE方法论，将错误内容与通道特异性安慰剂（频道特定安慰剂）配对，包括内容消融（content-ablated）形式和SHA乱序（SHA-deranged）安慰剂。在提示通道（prompt channel）和权重通道（weight channel，小数据适配器训练）上评估0.5-1.5B的冻结小代码模型，每个臂-单元对生成4次。

Result: 提示通道：内容消融安慰剂组解锁12单元，实时错误模式臂解锁10单元（40单元抗性带），结果为机制无效（mechanism-null）。权重通道：错误内容适配器与无干预基线8-8平局（p=1.0），SHA乱序安慰剂适配器领先10次解锁，未确认内容归属优势。结果不构成等效性或非劣效性证据。

Conclusion: 模型并未将错误作为外部证伪信息用于产生新猜想，而是将来自oracle的表征写回生成状态中，使"测试"被"条件化"所取代。PoPE被提出作为一种安慰剂对照、可复验的测量标准。

Abstract: Frozen small code LLMs are deployed locally, yet the information guiding a retry after a failed attempt is still measured without placebo controls in the self-repair literature. We treat a failed program as a conjecture and an execution counterexample as an oracle-relative refutation, and introduce PoPE (Popperian Placebo-controlled Evaluation): a methodology for measuring whether evidence that falsifies LLM-generated code can be used operationally by that same model. In PoPE, error content is paired with channel-specific placebos that keep the predeclared scaffold while ablating task-relevant content or deranging the task-error assignment. Frozen small code models (0.5-1.5B) are evaluated under preregistered rules through a prompt channel and a weight channel (small-data adapter training), with four generations per arm-unit pair. In the prompt channel, public-tier screening unlocked 12 units under the content-ablated form placebo versus 10 under the live error-pattern arm on a 40-unit resistant band; the result was recorded as mechanism-null. In the weight channel, an 8-8 tie was observed between the error-content adapter and the intervention-free baseline (p=1.0), while the SHA-deranged placebo adapter stayed ahead with 10 unlocks; content-attributable superiority was not confirmed. These results do not constitute evidence of equivalence or non-inferiority. Equivalence was not tested separately. Findings are restricted to the public-tier screening endpoint; hidden-tier confirmation was deferred by design. We read this not as compiled criticism disappearing as information, but as the loss of its external role in testing a new conjecture: when a representation learned from the oracle is written back into the generation state, testing is replaced by conditioning. No working JEPA-RL controller is claimed. PoPE is presented as a placebo-controlled, retestable measurement standard.

</details>


### [221] [Software Supply Chains are Dead: Use-Case-Oriented Regeneration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13021)
*Tanmay Singla,James C. Davis*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的软件来源范式——面向用例的再生成（use-case-oriented regeneration），通过AI生成仅包含依赖中实际被使用的功能代码，替代传统的外部依赖引入。实验表明该方法在180对仓库-依赖组合中保留了99.8%的行为，并减少了93%的API暴露面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统软件开发中"重用外部依赖"的假设正受到两方面挑战：软件供应链攻击提高了外部依赖的维护成本，而生成式AI降低了本地实现代码的成本。因此需要重新思考"构建vs.重用"的权衡。

Method: 提出面向用例的再生成范式：采用代理化工作流（agentic workflow），自动识别仓库中实际使用的依赖功能片段，仅合成这些特定功能的代码，而非引入整个依赖库。

Result: 在180对仓库-依赖组合上评估：替换后的代码保留了99.8%的仓库行为（通过基线验证检查），并将暴露的API表面减少了93%。

Conclusion: 软件来源策略将朝着可验证的、仓库特定的代码合成方向演进，尤其适用于功能狭窄、稳定且测试充分的依赖场景。

Abstract: Modern software development relies on an increasingly doubtful premise: that the up-front implementation savings from adopting a dependency outweighs the maintenance costs. Two changes are reshaping the build-vs.-reuse calculus: software supply chain attacks have raised the cost of external reliance, while generative AI has lowered the cost of local implementation. We envision use-case-oriented regeneration as a new software sourcing paradigm that shifts the supply chain from external trust to local verification. We evaluate an agentic workflow that synthesizes only the specific slice of dependency functionality that a repository exercises. Our measurements across 180 repository-dependency pairs suggest that this approach is feasible: the replacements preserve 99.8% of repository-observed behavior across baseline validation checks and reduce the exported API surface by 93%. Software sourcing may evolve toward verifiable repository-specific code synthesis, especially when the required functionality is narrow, stable, and well tested.

</details>

### [222] [Stop using Media Bias/Fact Check in research](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12108)
*Alejandro Javier Ruiz Iglesias,Julia Witte Zimmerman,Ashley M. A. Fehr,Peter Sheridan Dodds,Christopher M. Danforth*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 本文揭示了Media Bias/Fact Check (MBFC) 数据集在学术研究中被广泛使用，但其方法论并不符合学术研究的基本标准。MBFC的偏见、可信度和事实性评级实际上基于单一个人的观点，且其自身声明并非科学方法。研究呼吁学术界停止使用MBFC数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MBFC数据集被大量用于 misinformation 研究，但鲜有学者对其方法论进行严格审视。作者旨在揭示该数据集的根本性缺陷，指出其并非中立准确，而是对霸权的话语计算产物。

Method: 作者系统分析了MBFC的"About"页面声明，对比了学术论文中对MBFC的描述，指出这些描述常与MBFC自身声明矛盾。通过论证MBFC数据源于单一个人观点、不符合科学标准，揭示其作为研究工具的不可靠性。

Result: 未发现任何论文能充分描述MBFC仅是单一个人的观点，或批判性地参与其方法论以证明使用其数据的合理性。MBFC数据量化了政治过程（包括诋毁媒体的运动）的结果，并将之呈现为关于世界的简单事实。

Conclusion: 作者呼吁学术研究者停止使用MBFC数据，认为使用该数据集会复制 misinformation 研究本身旨在解决的危机。

Abstract: Media Bias/Fact Check (MBFC) purports to quantify the bias, credibility, and factuality of reporting for roughly 10,000 media sources, and the resulting data is commonly used in misinformation research. In the present study, we show that MBFC's methodology does not meet basic standards of rigor for academic research. Despite its widespread prevalence, studies using MBFC rarely examine it carefully, often describing it in ways that contradict its ``About'' page, or treating it as authoritative despite MBFC's disclaimer that it is ``not a tested scientific method... [but] a simple guide to the idea of a source's bias.'' We identified no papers that adequately describe MBFC as the opinions of a single person or critically engage with its methodology in order to justify proceeding with its use. We argue that MBFC's data is not neutral or accurate, but a computationally legible account of hegemony, a specious dataset for uncritical research that mistakes the familiarity of the concepts it quantifies with accuracy. Our study concludes with a call for academic researchers to stop using MBFC. MBFC's data quantifies the results of political processes, including campaigns to discredit the press, and presents them as simple facts about the world, thus reproducing the crisis misinformation scholarship exists to address.

</details>


### [223] [Context Distribution Restoration for Social Surveys: A Recoverability-Adaptive Transport Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12535)
*Lei Zhao,Fujin Huang,Ling Kang,Quan Guo*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 本文提出上下文分布恢复（CDR）框架，利用最优传输理论恢复不完整的社会调查元数据（城乡状态、性别等），在保持人口统计先验分布的同时平衡个体证据，在CHNS、NHANES、BRFSS三个大型调查中实现TVD<0.001且精度损失极小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 社会调查中关键元数据（城乡、性别等分层字段）往往缺失，但外部人口统计或调查设计信息可提供已知先验分布P(M)。现有分类器虽能恢复元数据但会破坏人口分布一致性，需一种既能利用个体证据又能满足群体约束的方法。

Method: 将问题形式化为上下文分布恢复（CDR）：从协变量X恢复样本级元数据同时尊重先验P(M)。理论上用互信息I(X;M)定义可恢复性，操作上通过校准预测不确定性近似。核心创新是可恢复性自适应传输机制，在最优传输框架内调节个体证据与群体约束的权衡。

Result: 在CHNS、NHANES、BRFSS三个大规模调查（最多67k测试样本）中，未约束分类器（XGBoost）精度高但违反P(M)（TVD≈0.11），而CDR将TVD降至<0.001且精度损失极小。CHNS案例研究展示了可解释的连续谱结构。

Conclusion: CDR为计算社会科学中人口一致的元数据恢复提供了有效框架，能在保持群体分布约束的前提下实现高精度个体预测。

Abstract: Social surveys such as CHNS, NHANES, and BRFSS underpin population health and inequality research, yet critical metadata--urban/rural status, gender, and related stratification fields--are often incomplete. External population statistics or survey design information can provide a known prior P(M) over metadata categories. We formalize this setting as Context Distribution Restoration (CDR): recovering sample-level metadata assignments from covariates X while respecting P(M). The core challenge is that metadata recoverability varies by case: some respondents carry strong signals in X, others do not. We define recoverability theoretically as mutual information R(M|X) = I(X; M) and approximate it operationally via calibrated predictive uncertainty. We then introduce a recoverability-adaptive transport mechanism within an optimal transport framework to regulate the trade-off between individual evidence and population constraints. Across three large-scale surveys (CHNS, NHANES, BRFSS; up to 67k test samples), we show that unconstrained classifiers (XGBoost) achieve high accuracy but violate P(M) (TVD approximately 0.11), while CDR restores TVD < 0.001 with minimal accuracy loss. A CHNS case study illustrates interpretable continuum structure. CDR offers a framework for population-consistent metadata restoration in computational social science.

</details>

### [224] [SkillComm: Skill-Driven Semantic Communication for Sequential Workflows via Incremental Token Transmission](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11972)
*Ziyang Meng,Lu Lu*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: SkillComm是一个面向有序技能工作流的语义通信框架，通过可复用的技能状态实现跨步骤记忆感知的令牌优先传输与重建，在Detect-Segment-Keypoint工作流中降低51.2%的传输成本，同时保持99.4%的高精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有DeepJSCC和提示引导视觉发射器将每个任务视为独立的全令牌传输，缺乏跨语义工作流的执行记忆复用，导致在Detect、Segment、Keypoint等工作流中效率低下，因为后续阶段通常只需要与状态相关的语义更新。

Method: 提出SkillComm框架，核心包括：(1) Skill-Book将高级视觉意图映射为收发两端同步的可执行技能序列；(2) 自适应令牌选择利用跨步骤记忆仅传输状态激活令牌；(3) 接收端结合解码令牌与本地历史记忆重建任务就绪的令牌网格。

Result: 在MS COCO 2017验证集上的Detect-Segment-Keypoint工作流实验中，令牌传输成本降低51.2%，在高SNR下保持99.4%的上界归一化平均精度。

Conclusion: 可复用的技能状态能够实现选择性语义更新传递，为未来具身智能和智能体视觉系统提供了高效的通信范式。

Abstract: As wireless visual intelligence evolves from isolated task inference to ordered skill workflows, the communication bottleneck shifts from transmitting a single semantic representation to coordinating reusable skill states under channel constraints. Existing DeepJSCC and prompt-guided visual transmitters usually treat each task as an independent full-token transmission, with limited reuse of execution memory across semantic workflows. This is inefficient for workflows such as Detect, Segment, and Keypoint, where later stages often require only state-relevant semantic updates. To this end, we propose SkillComm, a skill-driven semantic communication framework that uses reusable skill states as shared context for workflow-aware token prioritization and memory-assisted token-grid reconstruction. A shared Skill-Book maps a high-level visual intent into a synchronized executable skill sequence at the transmitter and receiver. Conditioned on this workflow, adaptive token selection exploits cross-step memory to transmit only state-active tokens through joint source-channel coding, while the receiver reconstructs a task-ready token grid by combining decoded tokens with local historical memory. Experiments on the MS COCO 2017 validation set for the Detect-Segment-Keypoint workflow show that SkillComm reduces token transmission cost by 51.2% while retaining 99.4% upper-bound-normalized average precision at high SNR. These results demonstrate that reusable skill states enable selective semantic update delivery for future agentic and embodied visual intelligence.

</details>


### [225] [OSNR/GSNR Prediction in Brownfield Links via a DLM-Anchored Hybrid Physics/ML Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12152)
*Agastya Raj,Venkata Virajit Garbhapu,Hiroyuki Ishihara,Peyman Pahlevanzadeh,Hideki Nishizawa,Takeo Sasai,Daniel C. Kilper,Marco Ruffini*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于数字孪生模型（DLM）的混合物理/机器学习框架，用于棕地光网络链路，能够精确预测每通道功率、OSNR和GSNR，校准后OSNR/GSNR误差不超过0.39/0.43 dB。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对棕地光网络链路中物理模型精度不足、传统校准方法效率低的问题，提出结合数字孪生模型与机器学习的混合框架，以提高每通道功率、OSNR和GSNR的预测准确性。

Method: 提出一个DLM锚定的混合物理/ML框架，通过数字孪生模型（DLM）校准光网络中的跨段/ILA边界参数，结合物理模型与机器学习方法进行预测。

Result: 在单通道和OSaaS（光业务即服务）场景下，OSNR预测误差不超过0.39 dB，GSNR预测误差不超过0.43 dB，验证了框架的高精度。

Conclusion: 该DLM锚定的混合框架能够有效提升棕地光网络链路的性能预测精度，适用于实际网络运维与资源优化。

Abstract: We present a DLM-anchored hybrid physics/ML framework for brownfield optical links that accurately predicts per-channel power, OSNR, and GSNR. Calibrating span/ILA boundaries via DLM yields OSNR/GSNR errors of no more than 0.39/0.43 dB across single-channel and OSaaS provisioning.

</details>


### [226] [High-Precision Hybrid FA-PSO Based Inversion of Building Material Parameters for Fundamental Wireless Performance Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12721)
*Zhuowei Li,Yalei Zhu,Hanqing Zhang,Sui Li,Meng Chen,Tong Zhang,Zi-Yang Wu,Dan Yang,Songjiang Yang,Jiliang Zhang*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 提出基于萤火虫-粒子群优化(FA-PSO)算法的反演方法，利用自由空间法估算建筑材料的介电常数、电导率和厚度，并推导了Cramer-Rao下界(CRLB)作为理论基准。数值结果表明，对于较薄材料，估计精度接近理论下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确估算建筑材料的电磁参数（介电常数、电导率、厚度）对于评估其无线性能至关重要，现有方法在收敛效率和鲁棒性方面存在不足，需要更有效的反演框架。

Method: 采用自适应萤火虫算法(FA)系统优化粒子群优化(PSO)的超参数，并优化高斯分布的种群初始化参数，逐步提高参数估计精度；同时推导了复高斯噪声模型下的CRLB作为理论基准。

Result: 对于较薄材料，FA-PSO算法的估计精度接近Cramer-Rao理论下界，验证了反演框架的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究准确提取了建筑材料的电磁特性，为评估其无线性能提供了有力支持。

Abstract: In this paper, we propose an inversion method based on the firefly particle swarm optimization (FA-PSO) algorithm to estimate the permittivity, conductivity, and thickness of building materials using the free-space method. To improve convergence efficiency and robustness, an adaptive firefly algorithm (FA) is employed to systematically optimize the hyperparameters of the particle swarm optimization (PSO). By optimizing the parameters of the Gaussian distribution used for population initialization, the accuracy of parameter estimation is gradually improved. Furthermore, we derive the Cramer-Rao lower bound (CRLB) for the permittivity, conductivity, and thickness under a complex Gaussian noise model, which serves as a theoretical benchmark for evaluating the estimation accuracy of the FA-PSO algorithm. Numerical results indicate that for relatively thin materials, the estimation accuracy of the proposed method approaches this theoretical lower bound, confirming the effectiveness of the inversion framework. This study accurately extracts the electromagnetic properties of building materials, providing strong support for evaluating their wireless performance.

</details>
